_
 
##
 ato yathāsambhavaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo grāhyaḥ 
_
 kvacit saṃyogaḥ 
_
 kvacit samavāya iti 
_
 tathā cābhāve 'pi viśeṣacakṣurādisambandha eva viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ 
_
 tena satā ca viśiṣṭapratyayajananāt 
_
 na cādṛṣṭasyātra kāraṇatvaṃ niṣidhyate 
_
 sakalakāryeṣu sādhāraṇatvāt 
_
 nāpyadṛṣṭo dṛṣṭakāraṇaṃ pratyāvadhe 
_
 śarīrāderapyabhāvaprasaṅgāt 
_
 tathāhi sukhādi sampādakodṛṣṭa evāstvalaṃ śarīrādiparikalpanayeti 
_
 athādṛṣṭasadbhāvepi śarīrādayo dṛṣṭatvādabhyupagamyante 
_
 tarhi viśeṣyacakṣurādisambandha eva dṛṣṭatvād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣya bhāvo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ 
_
 
##
 atha viśeṣaṇe tasyāvṛttaḥ kathaṃ tadbhāva iti cet 
_
 na 
_
 adṛṣṭvad vyāpārāpekṣayā tada vṛttitvāt 
_
 athaikajñānālambanale surabhi dravyam iti vibhinnendriyagrāhyayoviśeṣaṇaviśeṣya bhāvo na syāt 
_
 na hi vibhinnendriyābhyāmekaṃ vijñāna sampādyaṃ dṛṣṭamitiḥ 
_
 na 
_
 viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayovibhinnajñānālambanale bādhakopapatteranusandhānajñānametat 
_
 tathā hi prāṇena mandhamupalabhya cakṣuṣā sparśanena vā vravyaṃ paścānmanasānusaṃdhatte surabhi dravyam iti 
_
 na ca sarva viśeṣyajñānamanusandhānajñānamiti vācyama 
_
 tatra hi bādhakānupapatteḥ 
_
 tathā viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayovibhinnajñānālambanatāyām ekadaṇḍinamahamadrākṣam iti smaraṇa na syāt 
_
 tasya hi anubhavarūpatvāt 
_
 
##
atha puruṣapratyayasāmānādhikaraṇyād daṇḍinamānaya ityādiprayogeṣu puruṣasyaka kriyāsambandhāt
tadālambanameva viśeṣyajñānamiti cet
_
 na 
_
 puruṣasya viśeṣyatayā prādhānyāt kriyāsambandhaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyacopapadyata evetyalamativistareṇa 
_
 banye tvekajñānālambanatve viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo na syāt 
_
 tayoḥ karaṇakarma matvāviti manyante 
_
 tathāhi viśiṣyate 'neneti viśeṣaṇaṃ karaṇam 
_
 viśeṣyata iti viśeṣyaṃ karma 
_
 taccaikajñānālambanatāyāṃ na syādubhayoḥ karmatvāditi 
_
 nāyanātavyāpāre sahakāritvāviśeṣāccakṣurādibhyo viśeṣaḥ syāditi tajjñānaṃ kalpyate 
_
 yadi ca daṇḍatvaviśiṣṭo daṇḍaḥ puruṣasya viśeṣaṇamiṣyeta tasyāpyanya dityanavasthā 
_
 daṇḍaśced daṇḍatvasya viśeṣaṇamitaretarāśrayatvañca syāditi viśeṣya brānābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 asti ca viśeṣyajñānamiti tadanyathānupapatyā viśeṣaṇajñānamātra 
##
 yaccedaṃ viśeṣyajñānamutpatteḥ pūrvaṃ viśeṣaṇasya na tad rūpatāṃ darśayatītyuktam 
_
 tatra keyaṃ viśeṣaṇarūpateti vicāryam 
_
 na hi daṇḍe daṇḍatvādivad viśeṣaṇarūpatā pratibhāti 
_
 artha svānuraktaprathayajanakatvaṃ viśeṣaṇatvam 
_
 tacca yadi svālambanajñānasahitasya viśeṣyajñānajanakatvam 
_
 abhyupagamavyāghātaḥ 
_
 na caikavijñānālambanatve 'nurāgārtha paśyāmaḥ 
_
 tucchabdābhilapyatvādeḥ pratiṣedhāt 
_
 nāpi kramo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaheturanabhyupagamāt 
_
 viśeṣyajñānantu 
_
 viśeṣaṇajñānaṃ 
_
 darśayatyevānyathā hi tadviśiṣṭatvāyogāt 
_
 pacceda manumānādapratipatteḥ pratyakṣaphalakatvamiti 
_
 taccāsat 
_
 bādhakasadbhāvena atreka jñānālambanatvābhyupagamāt 
_
 na caivaṃ sarvatra bādhakamastīti 
_
 
##
 bale tu dhūmopalambhānantaramagnyanumāne satyagnimānayaṃ parvata iti jñānaṃ pratyakṣa meleti mukte 
_
 anyathā 
_
 hi ayam ityaparokṣatānirdeśo na syāt 
_
 atra ca sādhyā viśikṣāmiṇaḥ sādhyatve kathametat sādhanaṃ syāditi vācyam 
_
 yaccedaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ kimeko 'neko veti 
_
 tatraikatvābhyupagame 'pi na viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoravyavasthā 
_
 nimittāntarasyāsādhāraṇasya sabhāvāt 
_
 tathā hi viśeṣaṇaṃ svānuraktapratyayotpādakatvenetyuktam 
_
 viśeṣyantu viśeṣyajñānaviṣayatvena 
_
 viśeṣamamivaṣyabhāvastu para viśeṣyajñānotpattī sahakārī 
_
 na punarvyavasthākāraṇamiti 
_
 
##
 na ca saṃyogasamavāyāveva viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ 
_
 tayoḥ samavāye 'bhāve cābhāvāt 
_
 atrāpi viśeṣyendriyasambandho 'stīti cet 
_
 na 
_
 tasya viśeṣaṇāvṛttitvāt 
_
 nāpyadṛṣṭavād vyāpārāpekṣayā tavṛttitvam 
_
 saṃyogasamavāyayoranyatrānupalabdhaḥ 
_
 tathā hi saṃyogasamavāyayobadi vyāpārāpekṣayā viśeṣaṇavṛttivamiṣyeta 
_
 viśeṣyasambandha vimā amāvasamavāyayo graṃhagaṃ syāt 
_
 yatra hi tayovṛtistava mahaṇajanakalyopalo 
_
 adṛṣṭasya tvātmatāta syāpi sakasakāryotpatto sādhāraṇatvāt 
_
 saṃyogāvisadbhāve tadabhāve ca kevalasa yāmārobhyupagamyata eka 
_
 sa comavatra vyāpārāpekṣayā sambaddha isa sambo paramārthataḥ 
_
 
##
 na copacaritasyendriyāsahakāritvam 
_
 aparokṣaśānasyānyathāsambhavena tadabhāva siddhaḥ 
_
 dṛṣṭaśca śrotrānyopacaritasyāpi śabdajñānasahakāritvamiti 
_
 yaccedaṃ purabhi dravyam' ityādyanusandhānajñānamityuktam 
_
 tadasat 
_
 anyatrāpyevaṃ prasaṅgāt 
_
 na cātra vibhinnaśāmālambanave kiñcid bādhakamastīti tadeṣābhyupeyam 
_
 
##
 nāpi daṇḍinamahamadrākṣam iti smaraṇānupāttiḥ 
_
 viśeṣaṇaśānājanitasaṃskārāma viśeṣyajñānasahakāripāḥ saṃskārārambheṇāpi tadbhāvāt 
_
 yaccedamekajñānālambanatve 'pi viśeṣyasya prādhānyāt kriyāsambandhaḥ 
_
 sāmānādhi karaṇyañca ghaṭata iti 
_
 tanna 
_
 prādhānyasyaiva vicāryatvāt 
_
 ekajñānālambanatāyāṃ hi ki kṛtaṃ prādhānyamiti cintyam 
_
 sāmānādhikaraṇyanvekajñānālambanatvāviśeṣe puruṣapratyarana na ca daṇḍapratyayeneti viśeṣaṇahetvabhāvaḥ 
_
 
##
 aya vibhinnaviśeṣaganimitavorekasminsarṣe vṛttaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam 
_
 daṇḍīti pratyaye daṇḍo viśeṣaṇaṃ puruṣe iti 
_
 na caivaṃ daṇḍasya viśeṣaṇatve 'nyad viśeṣatamastāra sāmānādhikaraṇyam 
_
 naitadevam 
_
anekasya prameyasya pratimāsābhyupagamāra daṇḍī' iti jñāne daṇḍatvādyapi prameyaṃ
pratibhāsata ityabhyupagame kathana sāmānādhikaraṇyama
_
 tathā sūtravyāghātaśca samavāyinaḥ śvaityācchvatyabuḍhe śvete buddhistatkāryakāraṇabhūte kāryakāraṇasvabhāve iti 
_
 
##
 na punarbhūtābhimānakumamāko mukhako sāmānupapatteḥ 
_
 nāma pratimāna pratyayaviśeṣaḥ 
_
 sahakārivalakṣaṇyenāpi bhāvāt 
_
 nanvevaṃ tarhi viśeṣaṇavat sambandhe 'pi jānaṃ kalpanīyam 
_
 taba badanusagasyāti   bhāsena cakṣurādivata magahītasyāpi vyāpārābhyupamamāt 
_
 nāpyabhedopacārād viśeṣaṇāviśeṣyabhāvaḥ 
_
 puruṣe daṇḍaḥ iti jñānānupapatteḥ 
_
 atha viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyañ ca sambandhaṃ laukikīṃ sthitim 
_
 gṛhītvā saṅkalyyaiva tathā pratyeti nānyathā 
_
 iti saṅkalanājānamiti cet 
_
 naitad yuktam 
_
 etāvato jñānamālāpasya sadbhāve pramāṇābhāvāt 
_
 tathā hi paraṃ viśeṣyajñānamutpadyamānaṃ dṛṣṭam 
_
 taccānyathā ca ghaṭata iti viśeṣaṇe 'pi jñānaṃ luptam 
_
 na punarjñānāntarasadbhāve pramāṇamastīti 
_
 
##
 na cedaṃ niriviṣayaṃ kalpanājñānam 
_
 arthānvayavyatirekānuvidhānāt 
_
 bādhakānupapatteś ca 
_
 tadevaṃ gṛhītasya viśeṣaṇasya viśeṣyajñānajanakatvāt liṅgādivyāpārānupalabdheśca pratyakṣatvaṃ kālasyeti 
_
 satyam 
_
 tathekajñānālambanatve 'pi yugapādipratyayā na kālasya liṅgam 
_
 tasyāpi viśeṣaṇatayālambanatvāt 
_
 amīṣāñcendriyānuvidhānena pratyakṣaphalatvādityalam 
_
 
##
 sarvakāryāṇāmutpattau kāraṇatvaṃ pratijñātamāha * sarvakāryāṇāñcotpattisthitivināśahetuḥ iti 
_
 utpattirātmalābho bhāvānām 
_
 sthitiḥ kramabhāvyanekakāryakartṛtvam 
_
 vināśaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ 
_
 teṣāṃ kāraṇamiti 
_
 atra tu yadyapi sarvakāryāṇāṃ heturityukte sarvametallabhyate tathāpyavāntaraviśeṣāpekṣayā bhedakathanam 
_
 
##
 atha teṣāṃ hetuḥ kāla iti kathaṃ jñāyata ityāha * tadvyapadeśāt * iti 
_
 tathā hyutpattau kālena vyapadeśo madhyāhne utpanno 'parāhe utpannaḥ iti 
_
 sthitau ca madhyāhnaṃ yāvat sthito parāhnañca iti 
_
 vināśe tu prātavinaṣṭo varṣānte vinaṣṭaḥ ityādi 
_
 kāraṇena tu kāryasya vyapadeśo yathā cākṣuṣaṃ vijñānam 
_
 mānasaṃ vijñānam iti 
_
 
##
 athākāraṇenāpi vyapadeśaḥ sambhavatyeva 
_
 mūrtāḥ paramāṇavaḥ daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti 
_
 satyam 
_
 tathāpi sambandhe sati vyapadeśopalabdheḥ 
_
 na cānyaḥ sambandho 'tra sambhavatīti kāryakāraṇabhāvo jñāyate 
_
 athāsti saṃyogaḥ 
_
 na 
_
 guṇakarmādervyapadeśyatāprasaṅgāt 
_
 asti ca tatrāpi vyapadeśaḥ pūrvāhne śabdastathotkṣepaṇam ityādi 
_
 
##
 apāyaṃ vyapadeśaḥ saṃyuktasamakāyāda bhaviṣyatītimā prabhāva māvāsaṅgāt 
_
 ataḥ kāryakāraṇabhāva eka sambandho 'bhyupeyaḥ 
_
 tasya hi vyāpakatvāditi 
_
 tathā niyatakāle kusumādeḥ kāryasyopalambho na kālāntare ityasvayavyatirekābhyāṃ tasya kāraṇatvaṃ vijñāyate 
_
 tathā hi vasantasamaya eva pāṭalādikusumānīmudgamo na kālāntare ityevaṃ kāyontareṣvayūhyam 
_
 tathā prasavakālamapemate iti vyavahārāt kāraṇatvaṃ kālasya 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 sahakāriṇamapekṣyopalaḥ 
_
 kālasyā sahakāritāmantareṇa 'prasato arya vyavahāro na syāt 
_
 
##
tathā na paraṃ yugapadādipratyayahetuḥ kṣaṇalavanimeṣakāṣṭhākalā muhūrtabāmāhorātrā
rdhamāsamāsarvayanasaṃvatsarayugakalpamanvantarapralayamahāpralayavyavahārahetuḥ * iti
_
 tathāhi paramāṇoścāvaruddhanabhodeśatyāgopalakṣitaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ 
_
 tad dvayaṃ lava ityukto nimeṣaśca labadvayam 
_
 kāṣṭhā nimeṣāḥ pañcadaśa ceha prakīrtitāḥ 
_
 triṃśat kāṣṭhāḥ kalā proktā kalāḥ triśanmuhūrtakaḥ 
_
 ityevaṃ māsāderapi lakṣaṇaṃ prasiddha prāhyam 
_
 
##
 sa cāyaṃ kṣaṇādivyavahāro viśiṣṭatvād viśiṣṭaṃ nimittamākṣipati 
_
 nācāya nimittaṃ sambhavatīti 
_
 kriyādeḥ pratiṣedhād iti kālasadbhāvasiddhiḥ 
_
 tasya samavāmitva guṇavattvapratipādanārtha * tasya guṇāḥ saṃkhyāparimāṇapṛthaktvasaṃyogavibhāgāti vākyam 
_
 atra keṣāñcidutpattī samavāyikāraṇam 
_
 etairguṇairguṇavān kāla iti 
_
 
##
 atha dravyatvādeva saṃkhyāsadbhāvasiddhau kimeko 'neko veti saṃśayastannirāsāyahi * kālaliṅgāviśeṣādekatvaṃ siddham iti 
_
 kālasya yalliṅga yugapadādipratyayarūpaṃ taviśiṣṭamiti nānātvāpratipādakam 
_
 nanu cāsiddhametat 
_
 yugapadādipratyayānā paraspara viśiṣṭatvāt 
_
 ma ca kāryavailakṣaṇyaṃ kāraṇavailakṣaṇyaṃ vinā bhavatīti 
_
 nānātvameva nyāyyam 
_
 satyam 
_
 kāryavelakṣaṇyād vijñāyata eva sāmagrīvalakṣaṇyam 
_
 tacca sahakāryantarā nupraveśenāpi ghaṭata 
_
 iti 
_
 kathaṃ kālasya nānātvam 
_
 uktañcātra viśiṣṭakriyopacitasya viśiṣṭapratyayajanakatvamiti 
_
 na caivaṃ paramāṇūnāṃ cāturvidhyaṃ vyāhanyata iti pūrvavada vācyam 
_
 tadevaṃ nānātve pramāṇābhāvād dravyasya ca saṃkhyeyatvādityekatvaṃ siddham 
_
 
##
 tathā tadamuvidhānāt pṛthaktvam iti 
_
 tenaikatvenānuvidhānaṃ sāhacaryāt 
_
 yatra hokatvaṃ tatrāvaśyamekapṛthaktvaṃ bhaviṣyatīti 
_
 na caivaṃ parimāṇaviśeṣeṇa sāhaparyamastīti sānārtha kramātikrameṇa pṛthaktvanirūpaṇamiti 
_
 tathā * kāraṇe kāla iti vacanāt paramamahat parimāṇam * iti 
_
 yugapadādi pratyayānā kāraṇe kālākhyā iti sūtraṃ darśayati 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 yugapadādi pratyayānāṃ kāraṇe kāla ityākhyā saṃjñeti 
_
 te ca pratyayāḥ sarvatra bhavantīti vyāpakatvaṃ kālasya 
_
 tasmācca paramamahattvamiti 
_
 yad vā aṇuparimāṇānadhikaraṇatve sati nityadravya tvāt paramamahattvamiti pūrvavad vācyam 
_
 
##
 tathā * kāraṇaparatvādivacanāt saṃyogaḥ * iti 
_
 kāraṇaparatvāt kāraṇāpara tvācca kārye paratvāparatve iti sūtraṃ darśayati 
_
 kāraṇaparatvaṃ hi kālapiṇḍasaṃyogaḥ paratvotpādakatvādupacāreṇa vivakṣita iti vakṣyāmaḥ paratvaparīkṣāyām 
_
 tadvināśakatvād vibhāgaḥ iti 
_
 tasya hi saṃyogasya kṛtakasvādaśyaṃ vināśena bhavitavyam 
_
 sa ca sarvatrāśrayavināśābhāvād vibhāgādeva vinaśyatīti vibhāgaḥ siddha iti 
_
 atha kālasya kathaṃ dravyatvaṃ nityatvañcetyāha * tasyākāśavad dravyatvanityatve siddha iti 
_
 tathā hi guṇavattvādanāśritatvācca dravyaṃ kālaḥ 
_
 samānāsamānajātīya kāraṇāsambhavāccākāryatvena nitya ityatideśārthaḥ 
_
 
##
 nanu cātra kālasyakatāyo vartamānādivyavahāraḥ kathaṃ syādityāha * kālaliṅgā viśeṣādajasaikatve 'pi * ityādi 
_
yadyapi kālaliṅgāviśeṣādaasā mukhyayā vṛttyekatvaṃ siddhaṃ tathāpi sarvakāryāṇāṃ
prārambhaśca kriyābhinivṛttiśca sthitiśca nirodhaśceti tathoktāsta evopādhayaḥ
_
 tabhedānnānātvamiti 
_
 tathā ca prārambha kriyopalakṣito 'nāgataḥ kālaḥ 
_
 abhinirvṛttirātmalābhastadupalakṣitaśca vartamānaḥ 
_
 tathā sthiti kramamāvyanekakāryakarsavaṃ tadupalakṣito 'pi vartamāna eva 
_
 taspa yābad vastusad bhāvavyāpyatvād yāvad vivartate vastu tāvad vartamāna iti 
_
 tathā nirodho vināśa stadupalakṣitaścātīta iti 
##
 atha kathaṃ nānātvamupavaryata ityāha maṇivat pākavad vā iti 
_
 yathā mṇeḥ svarūpāparityāgenaivopādhimedādupacaryate nānātvaṃ pīto raktaḥ iti 
_
 tadihāpi bhinnakriyopādhivaśād vartamānādibheda iti 
_
 yathā vā svarūpāparityāgenaiva pulasya nānākriyāvaśāt pācakādibhedastadvadihāpīti 
_
 vāstave hi bhede bādhakopapatteḥ 
_
 tathā hi yadi vartamānādevastivo bhedo vyāpakatvañca syād ekasya vastuno 'nekakāla sambandhād avyapadeśyatā prasajyeta 
_
 na hi vartamānena vyapadeśo 'jītānāgatābhyāmapi sambandhāt 
_
 nāpyatītenetarābhyāmapi sambandhād avyāpakatvam 
_
 tarhi nānekasya puruṣasyakasminneva deśe 'tītānāgatavartamānapratyayāḥ prāpnuvanti 
_
 te tathā dṛṣṭāḥ 
_
 tathā caikasya vidyamānakriyopalambhādekasminnevadeśe vartamānapratyayaḥ 
_
 tatraivānyasya kriyoparamāda tītapratyayaḥ 
_
 anyasya cotpadyamānakriyopalambhādanāgata iti 
_
 kriyāvaśādeva nānā pratyayajanakatvaṃ na punarvāstavo 'sya bheda iti sthitam 
_
 
##
 idānī diśo 'vasaratrāptāyā lakṣaṇaparīkṣārtha dik pūrvāpādipratyayaliṅgā 
_
 ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 digiti lakṣyanirdeśaḥ 
_
 pūrvāparādipratyayaliṅgeti lakṣaṇam 
_
 tathā pūrvaścāparaśca pūrvāparo 
_
 tāvādiryeṣāmiti tathoktāste ca te pratyayāśceti 
_
 te liṅgaṃ yasyāḥ sā tatheti 
_
saṅgrahoktevivaraṇārthamāha * mūrtamavadhiṃ kṛtvā mūrteṣveva dravyeṣu viṣayabhūteṣve tasmānmūrtadravyādidaṃ
mūrta pūrveṇa dakṣiṇenetyādidaśa pratyayā yato nimittād bhavanti sā digiti
_
 tathā ca digitarebhyo bhidyate 
_
 pūrvāparādipratyayaliṅgatvāt 
_
 yastu na bhidyate na cāsāvevam 
_
 yathā kṣityādiriti 
_
 vyavahāro vā sādhyaḥ 
_
 
##
 nanu ca pūrvāparādipratyayāḥ parasparāpekṣitayā mūrteṣveva bhavantītyasiddhaṃ lakṣaṇā bhidhānam 
_
 naitadevam 
_
 parasparāpekṣitāyāmubhayābhāvaprasaṅgāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 yadi pūrvamapekṣya aparapratyayaḥ 
_
 aparacāpekṣya pūrvapratyaya ityekābhāve 'nyatarābhāvādumayābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 na ca ninimittaḥ 
_
 kadācidutpannatvādanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ mūrtadravyasya vyāpāropalabdhaḥ 
_
 agulyādivyapadeśāccālambanatvam 
_
 na ca tasyāviśiṣṭasya pratyayajanmani vyāpāraḥ 
_
 sarvatrāviśeṣeṇa pūrvādipratyayāviśeṣaprasaṅgāt 
_
 
##
 atha mūrtadravyamevāvadhibhūta nimittamiti cet 
_
 na 
_
 tasya sarvapratyayeṣvaviśeṣāt 
_
 tathā hi tasya nimittatāyāṃ yatrava pūrvapratyayastatraiva dakṣiṇādipratyayāḥ prasajyeran 
_
 aviśeṣāt 
_
 nāpi saṅketa eva nimittam 
_
 tasya hi nimittaṃ vinā sarvatrāpravṛtteḥ 
_
 tathā hyeka nimittaṃ vinaikatra saṅketitaḥ pūrvaśabdo nārthāntare pravartate 
_
 athāsti pūrvādi śabdānāṃ saṅketapravṛtteḥ kāraṇamekaṃ yatsadbhāvādarthāntare 'pi pravṛttiriti cet 
_
 sā tarhi digiti 
_
 athāviśiṣṭatayā diśo na viśiṣṭapratyayajanakatvamiti cet 
_
 na 
_
 ekatve 'pi viśiṣṭasaṃyogavaśād viśiṣṭapratyayajanakatvamityanantaraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ 
_
 
##
 atha vikalpajñānatvāniviṣayāḥ pūrvādipratyayā vāsanāvaśād bhavantīti cet 
_
 tanna 
_
 abādhyamānatvāt 
_
 abādhyamānaṃ jñāna niviṣayaṃ na bhavatyeva 
_
 śuklādivijñānavad viṣayasya cāṅgulyādivyapadiśyamānasyānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vyāpāropalabdherityuktam 
_
 na ca vāsanaivātra nimittama 
_
 tasyā bodhavyatirekeṇāsambhavāditi pūrvanyāyāt 
_
 ato viśiṣṭapratyayāḥ pūrvāparādayo na viśiṣṭaṃ nimittamantareṇa bhavanti 
_
 na cānyannimittaṃ mityādirūpaṃ sambhavatītyato nimittāntarāsambhavād yadā nimittaṃ sā digiti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyaṃ nyāyaḥ 
_
 sarvotpatto kāraṇatvaṃ kālavad draṣṭavyam 
_
 
##
 samavāyitvaguṇavattvapratipādanārthamāha * tasyāstu guṇāḥ saṃkhyāparimāṇa pṛthaktvasaṃyogavibhāgāḥ * iti 
_
 tatra cātideśaṃ karoti * kālavadete siddhāḥ * iti 
_
 tathā digliṅgāviśeṣād viśeṣaliṅgābhāvāccaikatvaṃ diśaḥ siddham 
_
 nanu pūrvāparādipratyayāḥ parasparaṃ vilakṣaṇasyaiva nimittasya pratipādakā iti nānātvameva yuktam 
_
 na 
_
 sahakārivailakṣaṇyenāpi pratyayavailakṣaṇyopapattirityuktanyāyāt 
_
 ato dravyatvādeva saṃkhyāyogasiddhau nānātve pramāṇābhāvād ekatvaṃ siddham 
_
 
##
 tenaikatvenānuvidhānāt sāhacaryādekapṛthaktvañceti 
_
 pūrvāparādipratyayānāṃ kāraṇe dimākhyā' iti vākyena paramamahattvam 
_
 tathā ca pūrvāparādipratyayāḥ sarvatra nimittaṃ vinā na sambhavantīti diśo vyāpakatvāt paramamahattvam 
_
 tathā kāraṇaparatvāt kāraṇāparatvācca paratvāparatve iti sūtreṇa saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ 
_
 tathā hi kāraṇaparatvaṃ paratvotpādako dipiṇḍasaṃyogaḥ 
_
 aparatvañcāparatvotpādako vivakṣita iti vakṣyāmaḥ paratvaparīkṣāyām 
_
 saṃyogaśca kṛtakatvādavaśyaṃ vināśītyāśrayavināśasya sarvatrāsambhavād vibhāgādapi naśyatīti vibhāgaḥ siddha ityatideśārthaḥ 
_
 tathā guṇavattvāda nāśritatvācca dravyam 
_
 samānāsamānajātīyakāraṇāsambhavāccākāryatvena nityatvañceti draṣṭavyam 
_
 
##
 athaikasyā diśaḥ prācyādivyavahāraḥ kathaṃ syādityāha * digliṅgāviśeṣādaja saikatve 'pi * ityādi 
_
 tatra hi yadyapi diśo liṅgānāmaviśeṣānnānātvāprasiddhī añjasā mukhyayā vṛttyaikatva siddham 
_
 tathāpi saviturye saṃyogā lokapālaparigṛhīta dikpradeśaiḥ saheti vibhakti vi pariṇāmaḥ 
_
 yad vā bhagavataḥ saviturye saṃyogāste keṣāmiti vivakṣāyāṃ sambandhasyāpi vidyamānatvād yuktava ṣaṣṭhī 
_
 
##
 lokapālaparigṛhītadikpradeśānām iti 
_
 anvarthā anugatārthāḥ prācyādi bhedena daśabidhāḥ * daśaprakārāḥ 
_
 * saṃśāḥ kṛtāḥ   paramaṣibhiriti 
_
 kimarthamityāha * śrutismṛtilokavyavahārārtham * 
_
 śrutiśca 
_
 smṛtiśca 
_
 lokaśceti tathoktāsteṣāṃ saṃvyavahārārthamiti 
_
 śrauto hi vyavahāraḥ vāyavyāṃ gavayamālabheta 
_
 smārtastu prāṅmukhye bhuñjīta 
_
 laukiko 'pi asmavṛddhāḥ prāṅmukhā yajante sma ityādivyavahārasya prasiddhyarthamiti 
_
 
##
 atha lokapālaparigṛhītadikpradeśaḥ saṃyogo bhagavataḥ kathaṃ bhavatītyāha * meruṃ pradakṣiṇamāvartamānasya * iti 
_
 pradakṣiṇaṃ hi yathā bhavati tathā meruṃ paribhramato 'pi viśiṣṭasaṃyogāstadvaśācca prācyādivyavahāraḥ 
_
 anvayavyatirekābhyāmupalambhācca 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 udayasamaye savitudikpradeśena yogāt prācīti vyavahāraḥ 
_
 tatra hi prāk prathamamañcatīti kṛtvā 
_
 evaṃ madhyāhnasamaye dikapradeśena saṃyopād dakṣiṇeti vyavahāraḥ 
_
 tathā cāparāhne tayogāt pratīcīti ca 
_
 evamudīcyādiṣvapi vācyam 
_
 
##
 nanvevaṃ tarhi sa evāditysaṃayogo 'stu pūrvādivyavahārasya nimittam 
_
 alaṃ diśaḥ kalpanayeti 
_
 na 
_
 ādityasyāpi pūrvāparādivyavahāraviṣyatve 'nyādityaparikalpanāyāmanavasthā syāditi nimittāntarameva nyāyyam 
_
 na cādityaparivartanaṃ sarvatra sambhavatīti tatra pūrvāparādivyavahārābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tasmādekāpyanekasaṃyogopacitā viśiṣṭavyavahārasamarthetyabhyupagantavyam 
_
 ato bhaktyā upacāreṇa daśa diśaḥ siddhāḥ 
_
 tāsāñcopacaritadiśāṃ devatāparigrahavaśāt punardaśa saṃjñā bhavanti 
_
 mahendreṇa parigṛhītā māhendrī 
_
 vaiśvānareṇa parigṛhītā vaiśvānarītyevamanyāsvapīti 
_
 
##
 idānīmātmano lakṣaṇaparīkṣārtham * ātmatvābhisambandhād * ityādiprakaraṇam 
_
 ātmatvenābhisambandhaḥ 
_
 ātmopalakṣitaḥ samavāyo vā lakṣaṇamiti 
_
 tathā hyātmā 
_
 itaramā bhivate 
_
 ātmatvābhisambandhād 
_
 yastvitarasmādamātmano na bhidyate na cāsāvālatvenālisambadaḥ 
_
 yathā vityādiriti 
_
 na ca tathātmā 
_
 tasmād bhidyata iti 
_
 vyavahārovā sādhyaḥ 
_
 tathā śabdārthanirūpaṇaparatvena pūrvavad vākyaṃ yojanīyam 
_
 tathā lāgasvākṣepapratisamādhānaṃ pūrvavad vācyam 
_
 
##
 nanu sarvametadasambaddham 
_
 ātmasadbhāve pramāṇābhāvāt 
_
 tathā hi na pratyakṣeṇo palabhyate spādivat 
_
 svabhāvānavadhāraṇāt 
_
nāpyanumānamastyātmapratibaddhamityāśaṅkayāha * tasya saupamyādapratyakṣatve
sati karaṇaiḥ śabdādyupalabdhyanumiteḥ śrotrādibhiḥ samadhigamaḥ kiyate   iti
_

##
 nanu cāyuktametat 
_
 ahamiti pratyaye tasya pratibhāsanāt 
_
 tathā ca sulyahaṃ 
_
 duḥkhyahamicchāvānaham iti pratyayo dṛṣṭaḥ 
_
 na cāyamanumāpūrvakaḥ

 liṅga liṅgisambandhānu smaraṇavyāpārasyāsaṃvedanāt

 nāpi śabdā 
_
 tena vināpyutpadyamānatvāt 
_
 nāpi viparyayajñānametad

 tadrūpatyāsaṃvedanāt

 tathāhi

 antaḥkaraṇaparicchedama

##
 namvevaṃ kṛto 'haṃ sthūlo 'ham iti pratyayastarhi kayam 
_
 mukhya pātrakopapatte 
_
 rupacāreṇa 
_
 tathāhi 
_
madīyo bhṛtyaḥ iti jñānavat madīyaṃ śarīram iti bhedapratyaya darśanād
bhṛtyavadeva śarīre 'pyahamiti jñānasyaupacārikallameva yuktam
_
 upacārastu nimita vinā na pravartata ityātmopakārakatvaṃ nimittaṃ kalpyate 
_
 bhātmani tu mukhyatvama 
_
 sunīti jñānena samānādhikaraṇatvāt 
_
 tathā hi yatra sukhīti jñānaṃ tavāhamiti bhānasyo palambhaḥ 
_
 sukhādiyogaśca śarīrādivyatirekeṇātmanyeveti vakṣyāmaḥ 
_
 
##
 yaccedaṃ rūpādivat svabhāvānavadhāraṇāditi 
_
 tadasat 
_
 ahamiti svabhāvastha pratibhāsanāt 
_
 na cārthāntarasyārthāntarasvabhāvenāpratyakṣatvaṃ doṣaḥ 
_
 sarvapadārthānāma pratyakṣatāprasaṅgāt 
_
 na ca parakīye 'pyātmani aham iti pratibhāsaprasaṅgaḥ syāt 
_
 tasyātmāntarāpratyakṣatvāt 
_
 pratyakṣajañcedaṃ vijñānaṃ na pramāṇāntaraprabhavamityuktam 
_
 na cātmāntareṇātmāntarasyāpratyakṣatāyāṃ svātmano 'pi tathābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 svasaṃvidā bādhyamānatvāt 
_
 nāpi rūpāntarasya saṃkhyā pratyakṣatāprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tasya pratibhāsābhāvenā pratyakṣatvāt 
_
 tathā yatra hi rūpaviśeṣasya pratyakṣatvaṃ tatraiva saṃkhyādayaḥ pratyakṣā ityuktapūrvam 
_
 
##
 athātmanaḥ kartṛtvādekasmin kāle karmatvāsambhavenāpratyakṣatvam 
_
 tanna 
_
 lakṣaṇabhedena tadupapatteḥ 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 jñānacikīrṣādhāratvasya kartṛlakṣaṇasyopapatteḥ kartṛtvam 
_
 tadaiva ca kriyayā vyāpyatvopalabdhaḥ karmatvañceti na doṣaḥ 
_
 lakṣaṇatantratvād vastuvyavasthāyāḥ 
_
 na cānayorekasmin dharmiṇyekasmiśca kāle kartṛkaraṇayorivāstu virodhaḥ 
_
 tathā hi svātantryaṃ kartṛtvaṃ pāratantryañca karaṇatvamiti tvanayovidhipratiṣedha 
_
 rūpatvādabhinne dharmiṇyasambhavo yuktaḥ 
_
 na caivaṃ kartṛtvakarmatvayoriti 
_
 
##
 ata eva madīyaṃ śarīram ityādipratyayeṣvātmānurāgasadbhāve 'pyātmano 'vacche dakatvam 
_
 śreharṣa devakulam iti jñāne śrīharṣasyeva 
_
 ubhayatrāpi bādhakasadbhāvāt 
_
 yatra hyanurāmasadbhāve 'pi viśeṣaṇatve bādhakamasti tatrāvacchedakatvameva kalpyata iti 
_
 asti ca śrīharṣasya vidyamānatvamātmani iti kartṛtvakaraṇatvayorasambhava iti bādhakam 
_
 
##
 na caikasminneva dharmiṇi kādivibhāgasyopalabdheravāstavatvameva nyāyyam 
_
 lakṣaṇa bhedasya vāstavatvāt 
_
 yeṣāntu lakṣaṇabhedo nāsti teṣāmeva doṣa iti 
_
kalpanājñānañca pūrvameva nirastamiti na kalpanā samāno 'pitā kāraṇādivyavasthā tadevaṃ
kādipravibhāgasya bhinnanimittatvādekasminnevātmanyanamānena pratyakṣeṇa vā paricchedya mānena tadeva kartṛtvaṃ na doṣāyeti
_
 
##
 nanvevamātmanyahamiti pratyayasya pratyakṣaphalatvāt tasya sokṣamyādapratyakṣatve satītyasambaddhaṃ vākyam 
_
 na 
_
 bāhyendriyavivakṣayā asyābhidhānāt 
_
 tathā hi kasmādātmā kṣityādivad bāhyendriyapratyakṣo na bhavatītyukte vākyaṃ sambadhyate 
_
 tasya saukṣamyād rūpaviśeṣakāryasamavāyasya 
_
 mahattvasyānekadravyatvasahacaritasyābhāvāna bāhyendriyapratyakṣatvam 
_
 tatra pratyakṣe 'pyapratyanābhidhānāllabhyate 
_
 tasmiśca sati karaṇaiḥ śrotrādibhiḥ samadhigamaḥ kriyate 
_
 śrotrādibhirityubhayatrāpi yojyam 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 śabdopalabdhiḥ

 karaṇakāryā

 kriyātvāt

 chidikriyāvat

 tasya saukṣamyād yathoktāt karaṇaḥ śrotrādibhirapratyakṣatve sati taireva liṅgabhūtastasyādhigamaḥ kriyate 
_
 
##
 śrotrādīnāmapi sadbhāvenumānamāha * śabdādyupalabdhyanumitaḥ   iti

 śabda sparśarūparasagandhopalabdhikriyābhiranumīyanta iti

 tadanumitāni tairiti

 tathāhi 
_
 śabdopalabdhiḥ

 chidikriyāvat

##
 athātra sarvagatātmaprayojyatve sādhye sādhyavikalatvam

 viparyaye vā siddha sādhanamiti

 na

 sarvānumāneṣu sāmānyenaiva sādhyasādhanabhāvopapatteviśeṣeṇānuvyāptyabhāve sarvānumānocchedaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 pramāṇaścānumānamiti vakṣyāmastadadhikāre

_
 tathā na paraṃ karaṇaḥ * śabdādiṣu prasiddhayā ca prasādhako 'numīyate 
_
 śabdādiṣu viṣayeṣu prasiddhivijñānaṃ tayā prasādhakaḥ samavāyikāraṇamātmānumīyate

 śabdādijñānam

 kvacidāśritam

 yo yo guṇaḥ sa sa āśritaḥ

 yathā rūpādiḥ

 tathā ca guṇo jñānam

 tasmādāśritam 
_

##
 atha śarīrādyāśritaṃ bhaviṣyatīti siddhasādhanamityāśaṅkayāha * na śarīrendriya manasām * iti 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 pare manyante prāṇavaccharīre sati bhāvāt 
_
 tadabhāve cābhāvāccharīradharma eva caitanyamiti 
_
 evamindriyādiṣvapyūhyam 
_
 tanniṣedhārtha na śarīrendriyamanasāṃ caitanyamiti 
_
 vyavahāre sādhye na sādhyāviśiṣṭo hetuḥ ajñatvāt 
_
 iti 
_
 yat vā svasiddhāntopadarśanametat 
_
 asmatsiddhānte nāmīṣāṃ caitanyamiti 
_
 nanvevaṃ yadi śarīrasya caitanyaṃ nāsti tarhi kimarthaṃ parairuktaścaitanyaviśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ 
_
 tathendriyabhāvavyatirekānuvidhānādindriyāṇāñcetyāśaṅkayāha * ajñatvāt * iti 
_
 na hi viduṣo bādhakamupalabhamānasyaivaṃ vacāṃsi pravartanta iti 
_
 tathā manyanta ebhiriti manāṃsi śarīrendriyāṇyeva 
_
 teṣāṃ na caitanyaṃ tatkaraṇānāmajñatvāta 
_
 acetanakāraṇā rabdhatvādityartha iti kecit

##
 atha karaṇānāmajñatvaṃ kutaḥ 
_
 kāryājñānāt 
_
 nanvevamitaretarāśrayatvam

 na 
_
 ghaṭādikāryasyācetanatayobhayavādisampratipatteḥ karaṇānāmajñatvaṃ siddham

_
 evamindriyeṣvapi

##
 śarīrendriyāṇāñca caitamyasyotpattāvanvayavyatireko kāraṇatvādapi sambhavataḥ kathaṃ tadādhāratvamiti 
_
 athaivamadṛṣṭakalpanādoṣa iti cet 
_
 na 
_
 pramāṇopalambhāt 
_
 tathāhi pratyakṣavadanumeyasyāpyarthasyāstyeva sadbhāvaḥ 
_
 tatra śarīrasya caitanyapratiṣedhārthamāha * na śarīrasya caitanyam * iti 
_
 atra tu caitanyasya pakṣīkaraṇe bhūtakāryatvamasiddha syāditi śarīrameva pakṣīkriyate

_
 paraparikalpitacaitanyaśūnyam

##
 anye tveka eva bhūtakāryatvāditi heturvivakṣita iti manyante 
_
 taccāsad bhūtatvādityuktenaiva vyabhicārābhāvāt

 atha bhūtakāryatvādityukte 'styātmanā vyabhicāra iti cet 
_
 na 
_
 tasya sādhyatvāt

_
 tathā kāryatvādityukte nāsti vyabhicāra iti vyarthameva syād bhūtapadam 
_
 na ca cetanayā vyabhicāraḥ

##
tathā * mṛte cāsambhavāt * iti 
_
 mṛtāvasthāyāṃ caitanyasya rūpādivadanupalabdherna śarīraviśeṣaguṇatvam 
_
 tathā hi caitamyam 
_
 śarīraviśeṣaguṇo na bhavati 
_
 sati śarīre nivartamānatvāt 
_
 ye hi sati śarīre nivartante te tadviśeṣaguṇā na bhavanti 
_
 yathā saṃyogādayaḥ 
_
 ye tu śarīraviśeṣaguṇāste tasmin sati na nivartante 
_
 yathā rūpādaya iti 
_
 na ca viśeṣaguṇatvapratiṣedhena sāmānyaguṇatvaprāptiā 
_
 pratiyogyapekṣitatvāt pakṣādi vyavasthāyāḥ 
_
 tathā hi caitanyasya pareṇa śarīraviśeṣaguṣatvameveṣṭaṃ tasyaiva pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate 
_
 na cātra śarīrasyaiva pakṣīkaraṇam 
_
 
##
mṛte cāsambhavāccaitanyasyeti hetoradhikaraṇatā prasaṅgāt 
_
 tathendriyāṇāṃ cetanyapratiṣedhaḥ 
_
 nendriyāṇāṃ caitanyaṃ karaṇatvād vāsyādivat 
_
 bhūtatvāt kāryatvādityapi draṣṭavyam 
_
 ito 'pi nendriyāṇāṃ caitanyam 
_
 tadupaghāte 'pi smṛti darśanāt 
_
 na ca guṇivināśe guṇasya sadbhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ 
_
 tathā hi smaraṇam 
_
 indriyaguṇo na bhavati 
_
 tadvināśe 'pyutpadyamānatvāt 
_
 yo yavināśe 'yutpadyate sa tasya guṇo na bhavati 
_
 yathā ghaṭavināśe 'pi paṭarūpādiriti 
_
 tathā ca smaraṇamindriyavināśe 'pi bhavati 
_
 tasmānna tadguṇa iti 
_

##
 yadi cendriyāṇāṃ caitanyaṃ syāt karaṇaṃ vinā kriyāyāścānupalabdheriti karaṇāntarai bhavitavyam 
_
 tāni karaṇānīndriyāṇi vivādāspadāni cātmāna ityekasminneva śarīre puruṣabahutvamabhyupagataṃ syāt 
_
 evañca sati devadattopalabdhe 'rthe yajñadattasyevendriyāntaropa labdhe 'rthe na syādindriyāntareṇa pratisandhānam 
_
 tatu dṛṣṭamato nendriyāṇāṃ caitanyam 
_
 yadi caikamindriyamaśeṣakaraṇādhiṣṭhāyaka cetanamiṣyeta saṃjñābhedamātrameva syāt 
_
 
##
 atha viṣayaguṇaścaitanyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti tanniṣedhārthamāha * viṣayāsānnidhye cānusmṛtidarśanāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 viṣayāsānnidhye tadvināśe vā anusmṛtirdṛṣṭā 
_
 na ca tadguṇastadvināśe bhavatīti

 atha manoguṇo bhaviṣyatīti tatpratiṣedhārthamāha * nāpi manasaḥ * 
_
 caitanyam 
_
 guṇaḥ 
_
 karaṇatvād vāsyādivat 
_
 yat kartṛmanastadapi sukhādyupalabdhī yadi karaṇāntaramapekṣeta saṃjñābhedamātrameva syāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 yat tatsukhādyupalabdhaḥ karaṇaṃ tadevāntaḥkaraṇam 
_
 yaccetanaṃ manaḥ sa evātmā syāt 
_
 atha karaṇāntaraṃ nāpekṣate 
_
 tarhi * karaṇāntarānapekṣitve yugapadālocanasmṛtiprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tayā hi manasaścaitanye yugapad rūparasasparśaśabdajñānāni prasajyeran 
_
 cakṣurādīnāṃ manaḥsambandhe sati karaṇāntarā napekṣāṇāṃ svaviṣayaiḥ sambandhāt

 tathāhi 
_
 smṛtiyogapadyañca karaṇānapekṣitvāt

 na caikasya krameṇa kāryajanakatvam

 tanna

 na hi karaṇaṃ pradhānakriyāśrayo dṛṣṭa iti 
_
 svakīyāpekṣayā tu sarvasya kartṛtvameveti 
_
 * tadevaṃ pariśeṣādātmakāryatvāt * caitanyasya 
_
 * tenātmā samadhigabhyate 
_
 
##
 kaḥ punarayaṃ pariśeṣaḥ 
_
prasakteṣu śarīrādiṣu jātyādiṣu viṣayeṣu caitanyapratiṣedhe tathā
tadāśrayasya vyavasthāpanānnānātvādhigamādākāśādīnāmekatvenāprasaktaḥ
_
 śiṣyate ca dravyāntaramiti pariśeṣaḥ kevalavyatirekyanumānam 
_
 tathā ca jñānam 
_
 kṣitijalajyoti rākādikkālamanovyatiriktadravyāśrayam 
_
 tavṛttau bādhakapramāṇasadbhāve sati guṇatvāt 
_
 yastu tadvyatiriktāśrayo na bhavati na cāsau tadvṛttibādhakapramāṇasadbhāve sati guṇaḥ 
_
 yathā rūpādiḥ 
_
 na ca tathā jñānam 
_
 tasmād vyatiriktāśrayamiti 
_
 
##
 nanu sarvametadasambaddham 
_
 kṣaṇikatvenāśrayāśrayibhāvānupapatteḥ 
_
 tathā ca padārthā nāmarthakriyayā sattvaṃ vyāptam 
_
 sā ca kramayogapadyābhyāmakṣaṇikeṣu na sambhavati 
_
 krameṇa janakatvam 
_
 ekasvarūpatvāt 
_
 yadeva hi pūrvakāryotpattau svarūpaṃ tadevottarakāryeṣvapīti sarveṣāmekatāprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 kāraṇavailakṣaṇyaṃ vinā kāryavailakṣaṇyasyāśakyasādhanatvāt 
_
 
##
 atha kāryavailakṣaṇyādeva jñāyate pratikārya pūrvasvarūpanivṛttāvanyadeva svarūpaṃ bhāvānāṃ bhavatīti 
_
 tarhi svarūpasyāvasthānānabhyupagamāt tathā'sattvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 athāvasthitasyāpi kramayogapadyābhyāṃ sahakāriprāptī tathaiva janakatvamiti cet 
_
 na 
_
 tasya tasminnatiśayādhāyakatvenātiśayanivartakatvena ca tayoravyatirekādanyatvameva 
_
 vyatireke 'pi tadbhāve 'pi bhāvasya kathaṃ kāryasya janakatvaṃ dṛṣṭamiti 
_
 na hyarthāntarajanma nyarthāntarasya kriyājanakatvaṃ dṛṣṭamityanupakārake vastunyapekṣeva na syāditi sahakāritvā bhāvaḥ 
_
 atha sahakāriṇāmapi sahakāryantarādhīnaṃ sāmarthyama 
_
 tadapi yadi sahakāryantarā dityanavasthaiva syāt 
_
 atha sahakāryantaraṃ vinaiva sahakāriṇāṃ svata eva sāmarthyamiti cedetaccānyatrāpi samānamityalam 
_
 
##
 tadevamakṣaṇikebhyo vyāvarttamānārthakriyā svavyāptaṃ sattvaṃ gṛhītvā vyāvartata ityasanto 'kṣaṇikāḥ 
_
 tadevaṃ bādhakopalambhāt parapakṣa evākṣaṇikaśaṅkāvyavacchedasiddhī sattvameva kṣaṇikasādhanamiti 
_
 tathā nirhetukatvād vināśasyotpattyanantaramevābhāva iti kṣaṇikatvam 
_
 nanu mukārādivyāpāreṇa ghaṭādivināśasyotpādopalambhādayuktameva tat 
_
 na 
_
 mātmabhāga saṅgatī tavyāpārāt 
_
 yadi ca hetorarthāntarabhūto vināśa utpāta tavā tadabhāvasyānupalambho na syāt 
_
 tatsvarūpasyāparibhraṃśāt 
_
 tathā abhāvasyaiva kāraṇa 
_
 kārya janakatvābhyupagame bhāvarūpatvaprasaṅgaśca 
_
 
##
 na cārthāntaratvāviśeṣāt tasminnupajāte kasyacid bhāvasyānupalambho na sarvasyeti viśeṣaheturasti 
_
 nāpi kāraṇāpekṣitāyāmavaśyambhāvaḥ syāt 
_
 vastre rāgasyeva sāpekṣitvāvaśyambhāvitvayovirodhāt 
_
 tathā hi vastre rāgaḥ sampadyamānaḥ kāraṇasadbhāvād bhavati 
_
 abhāve na bhavati 
_
 evaṃ kvacid vastuno vināśa ḥ 
_
 hetupratibandhād abhāvād vā vināśitvamapi syāt 
_
 yadi cāvinaśvarasvarūpāṇāṃ a hetuto vināśo gaganādīnāmapi nityatayābhyupagatānāṃ vināśaḥ prasajyeta 
_
 atha naṅa kṣorbhāvasya hetutā 
_
 tato vināśavat kiṃ tatkalpanayā 
_
 tatsvarūpatvādevāvaśyaṃ vināpi hetuṃ vināśo bhavatīti 
_
 
##
 yadi karaṇakāryatvañca syād vināśasya kṛtakatvāt tadvināśe 'vaśyaṃ bhāvonmajjanaṃ syāt 
_
 tasmāt na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavatyeva kevalam iti bhāvalakṣaṇasthitadharmānāśa iti 
_
 na cākṣaṇikatve pratyabhijñānaṃ pramāṇam 
_
 tasya kalpanājñānatvāt 
_
 tadetat sarvamaviditārtham 
_
 kalpanā nasya pūrvameva nirastatvāt 
_
 
##
 atha sa evāyam iti jñāne viruddhollekhād ekatvamayuktam 
_
 tathā hi sa ityatītākāraṃ jñānam 
_
 ayam iti ca vartamānākāram 
_
 na ca viruddhākārayorekatra sambhavo dṛṣṭa iti 
_
 tadasat 
_
 ākāravādapratiṣedhe pūrvānubhavajanitasaṃskārasmaraṇasahakārīndriyeṇa sa evāyam ityubhayollekhi jñānaṃ janyate 
_
 tasya cārthānvayavyatirekānuvidhānānni viṣayatvamayuktam 
_
 
##
 athāstu pratyabhijñānād avasthāyitvamarthānām 
_
 arthakriyākāritvantu katham 
_
 sahakārisānnidhye satīti 
_
 tathā hi krameṇa sahakārisadbhāve sati krameṇa janakatvam 
_
 pugapat sadbhāve ca yugapañceti 
_
 yaccoktam 
_
 ki tasya sahakāriṇā miyata iti 
_
 na kicit 
_
 kiṃ tarhi 
_
 sadbhāve kāryameva 
_
 anyathā sahakāritvāyogāt 
_
 yad vā tasya sāmathyaṃ 
_
 yā॑t kārakasākalyameva kriyate tatsadbhāve kāryajananāt 
_
 asāmarthyantu vaikalyaṃ nivartate 
_
 sākalyavaikalyayoḥ parasparasadbhāvasthitivirodhāt 
_
 na ca tayorāvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyāmarthasya tathābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tayostadvyatirekāt 
_
 
##
 na ca sahakāriṇāmarthāntaratvāviśeṣād aviśeṣeṇa sarvabhāvasahakāritvam 
_
 niyatasyaiva sadbhāve bhāvavyatirekābhyāṃ kāryajanakatvadarśanāt 
_
 nāpi sahakāriṇo sahakāryantarāt sāmadhyama 
_
 tamnirapekṣāṇāmapi parasparasānnidhye tatsamudāyasyaikakārya janakatvopalabdhaḥ 
_
 dṛṣṭaca caśūrūpālokamanaskārāṇāṃ parasparasānnidhye satyekakārya janakatvam 
_
 
##
 na cātretarādhipatyenānsyāvasthāyāmatiśayaḥ sampayata iti vācyam 
_
 bavyatireke sadabhāvāt 
_
 nahi sa eva tasyaivātiśayo bhavatīti 
_
 tathātiśayarahitānāmatiśaya janakatvamiti kāryāntare 'pi na bādhāsti 
_
 athātiśayayuktānāmatiśayajanakatvam 
_
 evaṃ tarhi teṣāmapyanyasmādatiśayaḥ sampadyata ityabhyupagame 'navasthāyāṃ vivakṣitakāryānutpatti prasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tasmāt sahakāriṇāṃ parasparasānnidhyamevātiśaya iti yuktamutpaśyāmaḥ 
_
 tadevaṃ kāryavailakṣaṇyaṃ sāmagrīvailakṣaṇyād bhavatīti na pratikāryam anyatvaṃ bhāvānām 
_
 
##
yaścāyamakṣaṇikānāṃ kramayogapadyābhyāmarthakriyāpratiṣedhaḥ sa viśeṣapratiṣedha syāvaśyaṃ
śeṣābhyanujñāyāṃ samartha iti prakārāntareṇārthakriyāprasaṅgaḥ
_
 na ca tadasattvagrāhaka pramāṇamastīti 
_
 tathā parasparādhipatyena kāryajanakatvābhyupagamāt 
_
rūpādīnāmekaikamanekarūpāde yugapat
kāraṇamityabhyupagame yogapadyapratiṣedhādeva tadantarbhūtaḥ kramo niṣiddha iti tasya svaśabdena punarvacanam punaruktameva syāt
_
 tathāhi yathā rūpaṃ yugapad rūparasagandhasparśānā rabhate tathā rasādayo 'pi 
_
 ekakavivakṣāyāṃ tatraiva krama ityekasyaiva pratiṣedho vācyaḥ 
_
 na caikamekasmādevotpadyate tadārabhate ceti niyamaḥ sambhavati 
_
 
##
 na cānyathaikasya krameṇānekakāryajanakatvam 
_
 pratikṣaṇamanyatvābhyupagamāt 
_
 tasmāt 
_
sahakārisadbhāve sati kramayogapadyābhyāmarthakriyājananād akṣaṇikānāṃ nāsattvamiti nāti nānātvamiti satvāditi hetoravyatirekaḥ
_
 na ca pakṣa eva tasya vyatirekaḥ 
_
 tasya smāntaratvāt 
_
 yaccedam akṣaṇikatvena virodhād bhāvatkapakṣa eva akṣaṇikaśaṅkā vyavacchedasikho bādhaka ityetadasat 
_
 virodhipratipattimantareṇa virodhapratipatterayogāt 
_
 athākṣaṇikastavirodhī pratīyata eva 
_
 sa tarhi pratipattirūpārthakriyākāritvād asanna bhavatīti kathamasyāsmād vyatirekaḥ 
_
 yadi cākṣaṇikaśaṅkāvyavacchedo bādhakādeva pratīyeta 
_
 sattvāditi hetovaiyarthya syāt 
_
 tasyāpyatadrūpavyavacchedaviṣayatvāditi 
_
 atha maulena hetunā kṣaṇikatvameva sādhyate 
_
 tacca yadi svalakṣaṇādibhinnaṃ kathamanumāna paricchedyam 
_
 tasya hi sāmānyaviṣayatvāditi 
_
 
##
 na ca sattvāditi hetoḥ sapakṣavipakṣābhyāmanvayavyatirekābhyāmantareṇa gamakatvaṃ nyāyyama 
_
 asādhāraṇasyāpi gamakatvaprasaṅgāt 
_
 sarvasya ca pakṣāntarbhāvāt sapakṣavipakṣā bhāva eva 
_
atha kalpanāsamāropitatvāt pakṣādivyavasthāyāḥ kalpanāsamāropite sapakṣe 'svayastadāropita eva vipakṣe vyatireka iti gamakatvam
_
 evaṃ tarhi kalpanāsamāropita pakṣādivyavasthāpekṣaṃ kālpanikamanumānamityavāstavaṃ kṣaṇikatvameva syāt 
_
 
##
 atha vināśasya nirhetukatvena kṣaṇikatvam 
_
 tanna 
_
 nirhetukatvasyāpi katipaya kālāvasthāyitvena 
_
 vināśe virodhābhāvāt 
_
 na ca nirhetukatvaṃ yuktam 
_
 bhāva ivābhāve 'pyanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ hetoyāpāropalambhāt 
_
 atha mudgarādivyāpārāt kapālasantā basyotpādaḥ 
_
 ma 
_
 tasya virodhyutpannatvāt 
_
 na ca kapālasantānastasyāvaraṇamiti 
_
 prāgiva tatkāle 'pyupalabhyeta 
_
 bāvaraṇatve 'pi tadvināśe tasyopalambhaḥ syāt 
_
 vaca kapālasantānena ghaṭasya virodhaḥ 
_
 tatkāraṇatvāt kapālānām 
_
 
##
 atha arthāntare vināśe bhāvasyopalambha ityuktam 
_
 tatra 
_
 tayoḥ sahāvasthiti virodhāt 
_
 tathā hi bhāve tūtpannebhāvasyāgrahaṇam 
_
 tatkāle tu bhāvasyeti dṛṣṭam 
_
 manvevaṃ ghaṭakāle tatprāgabhāvasya vināśe tasyāpyanyaḥ prāgabhāvastasyāpyanyo vināśa ityanavasthā syāt 
_
 tadbhāve 'pi na doṣaḥ kāryaniṣpatterdarśanāditi kecit 
_
 
##
 anye tvanavasthāyāṃ kila kāryasya parisamāptirna syāditi ghaṭatatprāgabhāva vināśayoreka eva prāgabhāva iti manyante 
_
 guravastu ghaṭakāle tatprāgabhāvasyānupalabdheḥ sa eva tasya pratiṣedhaḥ 
_
 prāgabhāvastu ghaṭaspati tayoḥ sahāvasthitivirodhāditi buvate 
_
 athābhāvasyārthāntaratvāviśeṣāt tasminnupajāte sarveṣāmanupalammaḥ svāt 
_
 na 
_
 tasminnutpanne kasyacidanupalambhena tayoreva virodhasiddheḥ 
_
yathā arthāntaratvāviśeṣe 'pi kiñcideva kāraṇaṃ kasyacideva kāryasya heturna tu sarvasyeti pratiniyamo dṛṣṭastakd
abhāvasya niyatenaiva bhāvena virodho dṛṣṭa ityadūṣaṇametat
_
 
##
 yaccedaṃ vināśasya kāraṇāpekṣitāyāmavaśyambhāvo na syāditi 
_
 vastre rāgasyeva sāpekṣitvāvaśyambhāvitvayovirodhāt 
_
 tadasat 
_
 ekatra vyabhicāreṇa sarvatra tathābhāvasyānu palabdhaḥ 
_
 tathā sāpekṣitve 'pi savitṛgrahanakṣatratārāṇāñcodayāstamayopalabdhenirapekṣatve ca udayānantaramevāstamayaḥ syāt 
_
 samarthasyopakṣepāyogāditi 
_
 avaśyañca uditasya saviturastamayo bhavatīti 
_
 
##
 athokta naṅa kṣu 
_
 kṣo bharbhāvasya vināśābhyupagame kiṃ hetuneti 
_
 tatra vinā 
_
 śātmakatvāsambhavādavaśyaṃ naṅa kṣu 
_
 kṣo vināśayogyasyaiva heto sati vināśo na gaganāderiti 
_
 tathā svakāraṇādityambhūta evotpanno bhāvo yenāsya avaśyaṃ vināśa hetunā bhavitavyamiti 
_
 atha tarhi kāraṇādutpadyamānatvādabhāvasya bhāvādaviśeṣaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tanna 
_
 svarūpa bhedasyopapatteḥ 
_
 yathā hi kāraṇādutpadyamānā rūpādayaḥ parasparaṃ svarūpabhedād bhidyante tathā abhāvo 'pi bhāvāditi 
_
 asti ca dravyādiṣaḍlakṣaṇālakṣitatvam bhāvapāratantryeṇa gṛhya māṇatvamabhāvasya rūpamiti 
_
 
##
 athotpattimattvādabhāvasya vināśe bhāvonmajjanaprasaṅga ityuktam 
_
 tadā 
_
 tanna sadbhāvadharmavilakṣaṇatvādabhāvadharmāṇām 
_
 yathā cānutpattimataḥ prāgabhāvasya vināśastathotpattimiṇo 'pi vināśasyāvināśa iti 
_
 na ca vināśavināśe bhāvonmajjanama 
_
 tasya atadrūpatvād atatkāraṇatvācca 
_
 tathā hi ghaṭavināśavināśo na ghaṭarūpo nāpi tatkāraṇamiti kathaṃ tasyonmajjanaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 na ca bhāvasyāsattvam 
_
 pratyakṣādipramāṇeyaṃvasīyamānatvāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 iha bhūtale ghaṭo nāsti iti jñānamindriyabhāvavyatirekānuvidhānād indriyajam 
_
 na ca niviṣayaḥ 
_
 ghaṭābhāvaviśiṣṭabhūtalālambanatvāt 
_
 
##
 atha ghaṭaviviktabhūtalopalamma eka ghaṭānupalambho nābhāvāditi cet 
_
 avyatireke tu ghaṭāvaṭho 'pi bhūtale svānāstīti jñānam 
_
 tasmād ghaṭābhāvopalambha eva ghaṭasyā nupalammo nopalambhābhāvamātramiti 
_
 na ca vināśānabhyupagame bhāvasva prāgina paścādapyavasthānād anupalambho ghaṭate 
_
 atha kṣaṇasthāyitvādeva dvitīyakṣaṇe tasyānava sthānamiti 
_
 tarhi sa eva tasyābhāvo yatsadbhāve dvitīyakṣaṇe tasyānupalambha iti 
_
 anyathā hīndriyādestādavasthyād vināśābhāve nityasyānupalambho na syāt 
_
 
##
 yaccedaṃ na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavatyeva kevalam iti unmattabhāṣitametat 
_
 anutpannavināśasya pūrvamapyupalambho na syād vinaṣṭatvādeva 
_
 abhāvena cāvirodha paścādapyavasthānamiti nityatvaṃ syāt 
_
 tathā kṣaṇikatve satyanubhaviturvinaṣṭatvādanyasya smaraṇaṃ na syāt 
_
 na hi devadattānubhūte 'rthe yajñadattasya smaraṇamiti 
_
 
##
 atha nānāsantāneṣu kāryakāraṇabhāvasyābhāvād asmaraṇam 
_
ekaśca santāne buddhīnāmasti kāryakāraṇabhāva ityāhitasakalapūrvavāsanākaṃ
kāryajñānamutpadyate iti kārakānubhūte 'rthe tasya smaraṇaṃ yuktameva
_
 naitadevam 
_
 kāryakāraṇabhāve 'pi nānātvastha tādavasthyād devadattādisantāneṣviva kathaṃ syāt smaraṇam 
_
 na ca santānasabhāve pramāṇamasti 
_
 buddherbudayantarakāryatve pramāṇābhāvāt 
_
 
##
 athāsti 'bodhād baudharūpatā' iti cet 
_
 tathāhi bodharūpaṃ kārya bodhādeva bhavati yathā śuklācchuklamityādi 
_
 nanvaivaṃ tarhi dhūmasyāgnijanyatvaṃ na syāt 
_
 samānajātīyasya dhūmakṣaṇasya bhāvāt 
_
 atha vilakṣaṇādapyagnikṣaṇād dhūmasyotpattiriṣyeta 
_
 bodhasyāpi vilakṣaṇāccharīrāderutpattirbhaviṣyatīti na bodhāntarasadabhāve pramāṇamasti 
_
 atha kiñcitsadṛśatayā agnidhūmasya kāraṇaṃ tadā jñānotpattau śarīrādāvapi samānam 
_
 tathā kṛṣṇādapi śuklasyotpattirbhavet kiñcit sādṛśyasabhāvāt 
_
 
##
atyantasamānajātīyañca samanantarakāraṇamityabhyupagamyamāne rūpajñānādeva rūpajñāna rasajñānādeva rasajñānaṃ
sukhādeva sukhaṃ duḥkhādeva duḥkhamiti santānānantya syānna cāsti saṃvedanamiti
_
 athaiteṣāṃ yugapadasaṃvedanam ananubhūyamānakṣaṇānāmutpattaḥ 
_
 tarhi tena vinā tasyānutpattestatsantāno 'pyabhyupagantavyaḥ 
_
 tathā ca sati tadeva teṣāṃ saṃvedanañceti prāptam 
_
 na caitadasti 
_
 tasmānna sarvaṃ jñānaṃ jñānāntarajanyamiti pratibandho 'sti 
_
 
##
 na ca vināśasyāvyatirekā anubhavasyāvasthāne smaraṇaṃ yuktam 
_
 atha dvitīyakṣaṇe tasyānubhavasyābhāvād anavasthānamiti cet 
_
 na 
_
 avyatireke hi tenāvirodhād avasthānameva 
_
 vyatireke tu sahāvasthitivirodhābhyupagamesmadarśanānupraveśaḥ 
_
 tasmāt smaraṇamavasthitamātmānaṃ prasādhayatīti 
_
 na ca kṣaṇikatve sati kāryakāraṇabhāvo ghaṭate 
_
 tathā ca yadaiva kāryasyotpāda stadaiva kāraṇasya vināśaḥ 
_
 sa cotpādānna bhidyata ityabhyupagame sahotpannayorna syāt kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ savyetarayoviṣāṇayoriva 
_
 vinaśyadavasthañca kāraṇamiṣṭaṃ vaiśeṣikaḥ 
_
 vināśasya hetumattvāt 
_
 
##
 nirhetukavināśavādinācca bhāvavināśavyatirekeṇa vinaśyadavasthānaṃ sambhavatyeva tasya vināśakāraṇasākalyarūpatvāt 
_
 nāpi svasaṃvidvādinaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇamasti 
_
 kāraṇasaṃvidaḥ svātmanyeva paryavasānāt 
_
 tathā kāryasaṃvidopīti 
_
 na kāraṇajñānaṃ kāryasattāmanubhavati tatsattākāle tasyātītatvāt 
_
 na ca jñānāntaramekaṃ kāraṇasattākāle kāryasattāṃ tadabhāve cāsattā vijānātīti 
_
 atha kāryakāraṇajñānābhyāṃ vāsanākrameṇāsti vikalpajñānaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvagrāhaka miti cet 
_
 tasyāpyetadrūpasamāropatvābhyupagame 'pramāṇavena kāryakāraṇabhāvasyāsiddhireva 
_
 tathāhi yad yatra samāropyate tat tatrāvāstavameva yathā śaṅkha pītādiriti 
_
 
##
 atha pūrvopalabdhānusandhāna vikalpamiti cet 
_
 evaṃ tarhi kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇaṃ vinā na vāsanā 
_
 tadabhāvāt tadadhyavasāyavikalpaḥ kathaṃ bhaviṣyatīti anubhavānurūpatvād vāsanāyāḥ 
_
 na ca bodhādanyā vāsanā sambhavatītyuktapūrvam 
_
 tasmādavasthitaṃ pratisandhātāramantareṇa tu kāryakāraṇabhāvasyāgrahaṇameveti 
_
 ayantu kṣaṇabhaṅgo 'smadgurubhi vistareṇa nirasta iti neha pratanyate 
_
 tadevamakṣaṇikatve satyāśrayāśrayibhāvasyopapattī satyāmetat pariśeṣād vijñānasyātmāśritatvamiti 
_
 
##
 tathā * pravṛttinivṛttibhyām ātmā jñāyate 
_
 kiṃviśiṣṭābhyām 
_
 * śarīra samavāyinībhyāṃ hitāhitaprāptiparihārayogyābhyām * iti 
_
 hitaṃ sukhamahitaṃ duḥkhaṃ tayoḥ prāptiparihārī tadyogyābhyāṃ tatsamarthābhyāmiti 
_
 vyāptipratipādanārthamāha rathakarmaṇā * sārathī rathasyādhiṣṭhātā tadvadātmā vigrahasya śarīrasyādhiṣṭhātā numīyate 
_
 tathā hi jīvaccharīram 
_
 prayalavadadhiṣṭhitam 
_
 jīvaccharorasamavāyihitāhita prāptiparihārasamarthapravṛttinivṛttyāśrayatvāt 
_
 rathavat 
_
 pravṛttinivṛttyāśrayatvaṃ vāyvādau vyabhicaratīti hitāhitaprāptiparihārasamarthapadam 
_
 tathā śākhāyantranipīḍitasya prāṇinaḥ śākhākarma ahitanivartakam 
_
 adhastanasya phalādiprāptehitaprāpakañceti tadarthaṃ śarīra samavāyipadam 
_
 tathāpi nadīsrotaḥpatitaśavakarmaṇā vyabhicāraḥ 
_
 tadapyadhastanasya śunastadupayogāt sukhaṃ bhakṣyata iti sukhaprāpakam 
_
 upariṣṭācca snānaṃ kurvatastapasvino durgandhatayā duḥkhaṃ janayatīti tannivartakañceti tadarthaṃ jīvaccharīrapadam 
_
 
##
 nanvevamapīdaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ vipakṣādiva sapakṣāderapi rathādenirvṛtti darśayatītya sādhāraṇatvameva syāt 
_
 na hi rathe jīvaccharīsamavetakriyāśrayatvamasti 
_
 atha jīvaccha rīrasamavāpihitāhitaprāptiparihārayogyā kriyā 
_
 prayatnavat kāryā 
_
 viśiṣṭakriyātvāt 
_
 rathakriyāvad iti 
_
 ihāpi na saviśeṣaṇasya hetoḥ sapakṣasadbhāvaḥ 
_
 tathā suptasya nāvārūḍhasya yathoktaviśeṣaṇakriyā abhipretena prāptihetuḥ 
_
 ahitena nivṛttihetuśca 
_
 na ca prayalavatkāryeti vyabhicāraḥ 
_
 tasmād icchānuvidhāyikriyāśrayatvaṃ heturiti 
_
 tathāhi jīvaccharīram 
_
 prayatnavadadhiṣṭhitam 
_
 icchānuvidhāyikriyāśrayatvāt 
_
 rathavat 
_
 kriyā vā 
_
 prayatnavat kāryā 
_
 icchānuvidhāyikriyātvāt 
_
 rathakriyāvat 
_
 
##
 tathā * prāṇādibhiśceti 
_
 prāṇāpānanimeṣonmeṣajīvanamanogatīndriyāntara vikārāḥ sukhaduḥkhecchādveṣaprayatlāścātmaliṅgāni iti sūtraṃ darśayati 
_
athātmanā sārdhamanupalabdheḥ kathameṣāṃ
gamakatvamityāha * śarīraparigṛhīte vāyau vikṛtakarmadarśanād bhastrāmāpayiteva * anumīyata iti
_
 vyāptipratipādanametat 
_
 prayogastu jīvaccharīram 
_
 prayatnavadadhiṣṭhitama 
_
 jīvaccharīraparigṛhīta vikṛta vāyvāśraya tvāt 
_
 bhastrāvat 
_
 vāyvāśrayatvamanyeṣāmapyastīti vikṛtagrahaṇam 
_
 vikārastu tiryag gatiśīlasya vāyoryadetad ūrdhvamadhaśca gamanam 
_
 tathāpi vāyuyvantareṇa pratihata avaṃ gacchatīti parigṛhītapadam 
_
 tathā hyantaḥsuṣiravṛkṣe chidrapradeśena praviṣṭasya vāyordhva madhaśca gamanaṃ sambhavatīti śarīrapadam 
_
 tathāpi śuṣkānubaddhaśarīre praviṣṭasya vikāraḥ sambhavatīti jīvagrahaṇam 
_
 
##
 nanvevamapi jovaccharosarihītavikṛtavāyvācavatvaṃ bhastrāderna sambhavatīti sādhanavikalatāprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tatra 
_
 bhastrāsādhāt 
_
 bhasvāśanena mahiṇīśarīrasya vivakṣitalā upacāreṇa 
_
 kyā himasmā māpyate prayatmavatā tathā mahiṣīśarīramiti vṛdhama 
_
 ataḥ sādhyasādhanādhikaraṇatvam 
_
 yaṃ vā jīpaccharīraparigṛhītavikṛto vāyuḥ prayatnavadadhiṣṭhitaḥ 
_
 jīvaccharīrapari gṛhītavikṛtavāyutvāt 
_
 bhastrāparigṛhītavikṛtavāyuvat 
_
 yathoktavikṛtavāyukarma 
_
 prayatnavat kāryam 
_
 yathoktasya vāyīvikṛtakamatvāt 
_
 bhastrāparigṛhītavikṛtavāyukarmavat 
_
 
##
 tathā nimeṣonmeṣakarmaṇā niyatena 
_
 iti 
_
 na vātadoṣādutpannena 
_
 * dāruyantra prayokteva * ātmānumoyata iti 
_
 vyāptipratipādanametat 
_
 yathā hi prayalavatādhiṣṭhitasya dātyantrasva nimeṣonmeṣakarma tathā jīvaccharīrasyāpīti 
_
 akṣipakṣmaṇoḥ saṃyogārtha karma nimeṣaḥ 
_
 unmeṣastu tadvibhāgārthamiti 
_
 tathā hi jīvaccharīram 
_
 prayalavadadhiṣṭhitama 
_

_
 vāḍyantravat 
_
 akṣipakṣmaṇī tu 
_

_
 dāruyantrākṣipakmavat 
_

_
 prayatnavatkārye 
_

_
 dāsyantranimeṣonmeṣakarmavat
