 ekasmādevārthapratītāvanyeṣāmuccāraṇa vaiyarthyāt 
_
 upalabhyate ca śabdād uccaritārthapratipattiḥ 
_
 atastadanyathānupa pattyā varṇakalāpādatiricyamānaḥ sphoṭātmā pratīyata iti 
_
 tathā gauriti śabdoccāraṇād abhinnākāraṃ vijñānaṃ śrotravyāpārādutpadyamānaṃ dṛṣṭam 
_
 na cedaṃ saṃśayaviparyayavyatirekādavayavijñānavad abhinnamarthaṃ vinā bhavatīti 
_
 varṇoccā raṇantu sphoṭasvarūpābhivyaktaye kriyata iti na vyartham 
_
 
##
 asadetat 
_
 pūrvavarṇānugṛhītasyāntyavarṇasya svānubhavasahakāriṇo 'rthaprati pādakatvāt 
_
 yathā ca 
_
 ekasmin varṇe jñānam 
_
 tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ 
_
 punarvi tīyavarṇa jñānam 
_
 tenāpi pūrvavarṇasaṃskārasahakāriṇā saṃskāra iti krameṇa antyavarṇajñānam 
_
 tasmāt pūrvasaṃskārābhivyaktāvaśeṣavarṇānusmaraṇe sati antya varṇādarthapratipattiḥ 
_
 na caivaṃ ghaṭādyanubhavajanitasaṃskārasya anubhavāntarasahakāriṇaḥ saṃskārārambhakatvenātiprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tatra viśiṣṭādṛṣṭābhāvāt 
_
 tadabhāvastu kāryābhāvenaiva jñāyata iti 
_
 atra ca kāryasya sadbhāvād viśiṣṭo 'dṛṣṭaḥ kāraṇatvena kalpyata iti 
_
anye tu śabdārthopabhogaprāpakādṛṣṭaniyamitāḥ pūrvavarṇānubhavajanita saṃskārāḥ pūrvavarṇeṣvekaṃ
smaraṇamārabhante tatsahakārī cāntyo varṇaḥ padam
_
 yadvā saṃskāramekaṃ vicitramārabhante 
_
 tasmācca pūrvavarṇeṣvekaṃ smaraṇamiti 
_
 
##
 anye tu pūrvavarṇānāṃ tajjñānānāñca atītānāmapi antyavarṇasahakāri tvam 
_
 anvayavyatirekopapatteḥ 
_
 yathā hi 
_
 vartamānasya kāraṇatvam anvayavyatire kābhyāṃ vijñātam 
_
 evamatītasyāpīti 
_
 yad vā pūrvavarṇavināśāstajjñāna pradhvaṃsāśca samīpatino 'ntyavarṇasahakāriṇa iti kṣīṇārthāpattiḥ 
_
 evaṃvidha kalpanānabhyupagame ca varṇoccāraṇavaiyarthyameva syāt 
_
 na ca sphoṭābhivyakta 
_
 akamuccāraṇam 
_
 samastavyastavikalpānupapatteḥ 
_
 na samastairabhivyajyate 
_
 samudāyānabhyupagamāt 
_
 na vyastaiḥ 
_
 ekenaivābhivyaktau śeṣoccāraṇavaiyarthya prasaṅgāt 
_
 atha kalpanā āśrīyate 
_
 sā arthapratipattāvapi samarthetyalaṃ sphoṭaparikalpanayā 
_
 abhinnākārañca jñānamantyavarṇaviṣayaṃ varṇatvaviṣayaṃ vā 
_
 yad vā ghanāvasthitipratyakṣeṣviva varṇeṣu bhrāntamabhinnākāraṃ vijñāna miti na sphoṭasiddhiḥ 
_
 śabdābhivyaktāviva sphoṭābhivyaktāvapi doṣā iti samānatayā śabdaparīkṣāyāmevābhidhāsyanta ityalam 
_
 
##
 vākyakalpanā tvekasmin pade jñānasyotpādaḥ 
_
 saṃskārasya saṅkatasmara ṇasya ca utpadyamānatā 
_
 tataḥ saṃskārasya saṅketasmaraṇasya ca utpādaḥ 
_
 padārtha pratipatterutpadyamānatā 
_
 padajñānasya vinaśyattā 
_
 tataḥ padārthapratipatterutpattiḥ 
_
 smaraṇasya vinaśyattā 
_
 padajñānasya vināśaḥ 
_
 saṃskārasya dvitīyapadajñānasya ca utpadyamānatā 
_
 tato dvitīyapadajñānasyotpādaḥ 
_
 pūrvasaṃskārasacivena padārtha jñānena saṃskārasyotpādaḥ 
_
 saṃskārāntarasyotpadyamānatā saṅketasmaraṇasyā pyutpadyamānatā 
_
 padārthapratipattevinaśyattā 
_
 pūrvasaṅketasmaraṇasya vināśaḥ 
_
 tato dvitīyapadajñānasaṃskārasyotpādaḥ saṅketasmaraṇasyāpyutpādaḥ 
_
 padajñānasya vinaśyattā 
_
 padārthapratipatterutpadyamānatā 
_
 pūrvapadārthapratipavināśa ityayaṃ nyāyastāvad yāvadantyapade jñānam 
_
 tena ca kalpanayā tatsaṃskārābhivyaktera śeṣapadārthaviṣayaṃ smaraṇaṃ janyate 
_
 tena ca svānubhavena ca viśiṣṭamantyapadameva vākyam 
_
 tasmācca vākyārthapratipattiriti 
_
 
##
nanu padajñānotpatteḥ pūrvam adṛṣṭavaśāt padapadārthaviṣayasmaraṇotpādābhyupa game tasya padajñānāt
saṅketasmaraṇakāle nāvasthānamiti padārthapratipatterūdhva kathaṃ vākyārthapratipattiḥ
_
 na ca padārthapratipatti vinaiva vākyārthapratipattiḥ 
_
 adarśanāt 
_
atha padajñānādūcaṃ kalpanayā tatsaṃskāreṇa smaraṇaṃ janyate tataḥ padajñānasya vinaśyatteti saṅketasmaraṇakāle tasyānavasthānāt
padārthapratipattya bhāve na vākyārthapratipattiriti dūṣaṇaṃ tadavasthameva
_
 
##
 asadetat 
_
 vākye saṅketānupapatteḥ 
_
 antyapadaṃ vākyameva 
_
 tad antyārthastu vākyārtha iti 
_
 yadā ca pūrvavarṇatajjñānādūrdhvaṃ kalpanayā tatsaṃskāreṇa smaraṇa janyate 
_
 tataḥ padajñānasya vinaśyatteti saṅketasmaraṇābhāvaviśiṣṭo 'ntyo vaṇaḥ padam 
_
 tadeṣā kākyakalpanā 
_
anyathā pūrvavarṇeṣu jñānadvāreṇa saṃskārād
vicitrasmaraṇānugṛhīto 'ntyo varṇaḥ padamityabhyupagamena padārthajñānānantara padajñānaṃ syāt
_
 varṇajñānavyavadhānāt 
_
 
##
anye tu pūrvārthasya pratisamādhānārthamantyapadajñānānantaraṃ
kalpanayā tatsaṃskāraḥ saṅketānubhavajanitasaṃskāraśca ekaṃ smaraṇamārabhate
_
 tataḥ padātha jñānasyotpādaḥ 
_
 padajñānasya vinaśyattā 
_
 smaraṇānubhavayoścāvirodha iti 
_
 tataḥ smaraṇānubhavaviśiṣṭād antyapadād vākyārthapratipattiriti 
_
 anye tu yadyapyantyapadajñānānantaraṃ saṅketasmaraṇāt padārthāvabodhe sāta padajñānaṃ vinaṣṭam 
_
 tathāpi punastasminneva jñānamutpadyate 
_
 tataḥ kalpanayā tatsaṃskārāt smaraṇotpāde sati antyapadād vākyārthapratipattiriti 
_
 
##
 asadetat 
_
 śabdasya viramya vyāpārapratiṣedhāt 
_
 ekadā padaṃ svaviṣaya jñānaṃ kṛtvā punarna karotīti 
_
 anye tu pratijñādipadasya padāntaroccāraṇakāle 'pi ākāśe padānta rambhakatvenāvasthānaṃ tāvad yāvadantyapadama 
_
 tataḥ pañcabhiḥ padaiḥ śrāpadeśe vākyam avayavibhūtamārabhyate 
_
 tato vākyārthapratipattiriti 
_
 nirastañcaitad anubhavana 
_
 na hi pūrvapūrvapadasyottarottarapadakāle sarveṣāñca vākyakāle 'nubhavo 'stīti 
_
 
##
 anya tu ekasmin pade jñānam 
_
 tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ 
_
 pudvitīyapadajñānam 
_
 tena prāktanena saṃskāreṇānyaḥ saṃskāra iti tāvad yāvadantyapade śānamiti 
_
 tataḥ prāktanasaṃskārābhivyaktī padacatuṣṭayaviṣaya smaraṇamutmayate 
_
 tadviśiṣṭañcāntyapadaṃ vākyamiti 
_
 na cātrānubhavena virādhaḥ 
_
 karaṇāṃśasyaiv kīrtanāt 
_
 
##
 anya smaraṇenānubhavasyāvirodhaṃ manyamānāḥ kalpanāmāśrayante 
_
 padajñānāt sakatasmaraṇasyotpādaḥ 
_
 padārthapratipatterutpadyamānatā 
_
 tataḥ padārthajñānasyotpādaḥ pūrvapadajñānasya vinaśyattā 
_
 dvitīyapadajñānasyotpadyamānatā 
_
 tato dvitīyapadajñānasyotpādaḥ 
_
 padārthajñānasya vinaśyattā 
_
 padajñānasya vināśaḥ 
_
 saṅketasmaraṇasyotpadyamānatetyanena krameṇa antyapadajñāne sati vākyārthapratipattiḥ 
_
 na cātra pūrvapadapadārthānasmaraṇena prayojanamasti 
_
 tatkāyasya vinaśyadaśānanaṃva kṛtatvāt 
_
 pūrvapadānurakte hi dvitīyapade jñānamutpannam 
_
 tadanuraktaṃ tṛtīyapadamiti aśeṣapadānuraktam antyapada vākyamiti 
_
 
##
 etaccāsat 
_
 pūrvapadānurāgasyāntyapade 'pratibhāsanāt 
_
 yathā hi 
_
 daṇḍīti jñānaṃ daṇḍānuraktameva 
_
 naivaṃ dvitīyādipadajñānaṃ pūrvapadānuraktamiti 
_
 na cāyaṃ niyamaḥ sambhavati pūrvapadānantarameva dvitīyādipadoccāraṇam 
_
 katipayakālavyavadhānapi uccāraṇe 'rthapratipattidarśanāditi pūrvaiva kalpanā nyāyyā 
_
 
##
 athāstvevaṃ vākyaparikalpanā vācakatvantu niṣidhyata 
_
 anyavyatirekābhāvāt 
_
 padārthabhyastu vākyārthapratipattiḥ 
_
 yatra hi pramāṇāntareṇāpi padārthaprasiddhistatrāntareṇāpi vākyaṃ vākyārthaprattipatirdṛṣṭā 
_
 yathā 
_
 paśyataścakṣuṣā rūpaṃ heṣāśabdaśca śṛṇvataḥ 
_
 khuranikṣepaśabdañca śveto 'śvo dhāvatīti dhīḥ 
_
 
##
 tathā ca dūrāccakṣuṣā śvetaṃ rūpamupalabhya heṣāśabdena vā aśvatvajāti manuminoti 
_
 khuranikṣepaśabdena ca dhāvanakriyāmavagatya vākyaṃ vināpi vākyārtha pratipadyate 
_
 satyapi ca vākye padārthānāmapratipatterna vākyārthaprati pattiḥ 
_
 yathā prasiddhapadārthaiḥ kaviiivaracite vākya iti 
_
 tasmādabhihita 
_
 padārthānām ākāṅkṣāyogyatāsannidhidvāreṇa vākyārthagamakatvamiti 
_
 na yuktametat 
_
 śabdasyāprāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt 
_
 tathā ca padarūpasya tāvad aprāmāṇyam 
_
 anuvādakatvāt 
_
 taduktam 
_
 padamabhyadhikābhāvāt smārakānna viśiṣyate 
_
 yaccādhikyaṃ bhavedetat sa padasya na gocaraḥ 
_
 
##
 vākyantu pāramparyeṇāpyavācakamiti kathaṃ śabdaḥ pramāṇaṃ syāt 
_
 atha padairabhihitānāñca padārthānāṃ gamakatvāditi pāramparyeṇa śabdaḥ pramāṇam 
_
tāha śrotraparicchinnasya śabdasyārthaparicchede vyāpārāditi
pāramparyeṇa pratyakṣasyāpi codanāviṣaye sannidhiprāmāṇyopapatteḥ kathaṃ
codanaiva dharma pramāṇam
_
 pramāṇamava codaneti nāsyāvadhāraṇasya vyāghātaḥ 
_
 vākyasyārthaparicchedakatvānabhyupagame ca pramāṇāntarāsambhavāt padārthānāṃ pratyakṣādiṣvantarbhāvaścintanīyaḥ 
_
 
##
 tatrendriyārthasannikarṣeṇa saha vyāpārānupalabdherna pratyakṣe 'ntarbhāvaḥ 
_
 avi nābhāvasyānupapatternānumāne 
_
 anupapadyamānārthāsambhavānnārthāpattau 
_
 upamānā 
_
 bhāvayośca niyataviṣayatvameva 
_
 pramāṇāntarasya ca anabhyupagamādayuktametat 
_
 na ca padānāṃ svārthapratipattāveva caritārthatvama 
_
 uktanyāyena vākyātha pratipattāvapi vyāpārāt 
_
 viramya vyāpārastu ekamarthaṃ pratipādya punastama pratipādayantīti pratiṣiddhaḥ 
_
 
##
 yaccedaṃ vināpi vākyaṃ vākyārthapratipattirityuktam 
_
 tadaparijñānāt 
_
 vākyena hi janitā vākyārthapratipattiḥ 
_
 pratyakṣānumānasampāditāḥ śvetā 
_
 dhāvatīti buddhayaḥ 
_
 yadapīdaṃ padārdhāpratipattau satyapi vākyena vākyā pratipattiriti 
_
 tadasat 
_
 pūrvapadārthasmaraṇānugṛhītasya antyapadasya vākyatvā avaśyamarthapratipādakatvamiti vyabhicārābhāvaḥ 
_
 anvitābhidhānantu na sarvapadānām 
_
 ekenaiva kriyākārakasaṃsargānvitasya padārthasyābhidhāne śeṣapadoccāraṇavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt 
_
 atha antyaṃ padamanvitābhidhāyakam 
_
 tasyāpi pūrvapadānapekṣitve taduccāraṇavaiyarthyam 
_
 sāpekṣitve tu na asmatsiddhāntād bhedaḥ 
_
 
##
 ke punaravayavāstadāha * pratijñāpadeśanidarśanānusandhānapratyāmnāyāḥ * vākyadeśatvāt 
_
 na punaḥ paropagatā jijñāsādayaḥ 
_
 teṣāmaśabdarūpatvāt 
_
 tata upadeśakrameṇāvasaraprāptāyāḥ pratijñāyāstāvallakṣaṇamacyate * anumeyoddeśo 'virodhī pratijñā * iti 
_
 anumeyaḥ pratipipādāya vārāṣṭatā hi astitvādyapekṣayā sarvapadārtheṣvastoti pratipipādayiṣita 
_
 yo hi dharmaḥ pratipādayitumiṣṭaḥ 
_
 tadviśiṣṭo dharmī pakṣaḥ 
_
 tasyoddeśamātraṃ sādhāvaruddhaṃ pareṣāma aniścitārthābhidhāyakaṃ vacanaṃ pratijñeti 
_
 apadeśasya vaṣayāpādanam arthaḥ prayojanamasyeti prayojanopanyāsaḥ 
_
 prayogastu 
_
 pratijñā tarasmād bhidyate 
_
 pratyakṣādyaviruddhānumeyoddeśatvāt 
_
 yastu na bhidyate 
_
 na pāsāvevaṃ yathā udāharaṇādiriti 
_
 anumeyoddeśo vā pratijñeti vyavahartavyaḥ 
_
 kānumeyoddeśatvāt 
_
 yaścaivaṃ na vyavahriyate 
_
 na cāsāvevam 
_
 yathā apadeśa iti 
_
 udāharaṇantu * yathā dravyaṃ vāyuriti * 
_
 
##
 nanu ca asādhanāṅgaṃ pratijñāvacanama 
_
 tadantareṇāpi sambandhavacanamātrādarthapratīteḥ 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 yad yat kṛtakam 
_
 tattad anityaṃ dṛṣṭam 
_
 yathā ghaṭaḥ 
_
 tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabda ityatra sāmarthyādeva pratijñārthasiddhayarthaṃ tadabhidhānam 
_
 atra ca prameyasya pramāṇenaiva siddheḥ sāmarthya kiṃrūpamiti cintyam 
_
 na pratyakṣa svarūpam 
_
 indriyārthasannikarṣaṇa vipratipattiviṣayasyāparicchedāt 
_
 evamāga menāpīti 
_
athānumānameva sāmarthya tadavaśyamarthapratipattau pakṣadharmatvādikama pekṣata iti
pratijñāvacanamantareṇa sapakṣāsapakṣāpravibhāge sati tadarthāpratītana gamakamiti
_
 atha abhidhīyamānānumānavyatirekeṇa anyadanumānaṃ prastutānumāna sāmarthyam 
_
 na 
_
 tasyāpi avinābhāvānapekṣitve na gamakatvam 
_
 pratijñāvacanacca vinā tadarthāpratīteriti pūrvadoṣānuṣaṅgāt 
_
 na cābhipretārthapratipādanāya anumānopanyāsakāle tadarthasiddhaye 'numānāntaraṃ paśyāmaḥ 
_
 
##
na ca kṛtakatvānityatvayoḥ sāmānyena vyāptyabhidhāne samarthasādhanasya śabda evopasaṃhārād
vijñāyate atraivānityatvam asyābhipretamiti
_
 sambandhābhi dhānasya viruddhāviruddhābhiprāyeṇāpi samānatayā vivekapratipatterabhāvaprasaṅgāt 
_
 atha yadyat kṛtakaṃ tattannityaṃ dṛṣṭamiti vyāptivacane viruddhavādī 
_
 anityatvena ca kṛtakatvasya vyāptivacane tattvavādīti viniścayaḥ 
_
 tanna 
_
 kṛtakatvanityatvayoppteḥ pratipādayitumaśakyatvāt 
_
 tathā ca 
_
 na kṛtakaṣu ghaṭādiṣu nityatvam 
_
 nityeṣu cākāśādiṣu kṛtakatvamiti dṛṣṭāntadoṣaṇa gatārthatvāt kathaṃ viruddhatvam 
_
 yadā ca nityaḥ śabda iti pratijñāya kṛtakatvā nityatvayorvyāpti brūte 
_
 tadā abhipretārthaviparītena vyāptikathanād viruddha vādyayamiti viśeṣādhyavasāyo bhavatyeva 
_
 
##
 nanu nityā nityābhiprāyeṇaivāpi nityaḥ śabda iti vacanasambhavāt pratijñā vacane satyapi tattvātattvavādinoraniścaya eva 
_
 na 
_
 vacanenaivābhiprāyaviśeṣa prasiddhaḥ 
_
 na hi vaktṛṇāṃ vacanādṛte 'bhiprāyāvabodhe pramāṇāntaramastīti nitya vacanānnityābhiprāya eva niścīyate 
_
 abhiprāyāntarakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇābhāvāt ' ata eva vādiprativādinorjayaparājayavyavasthā prāśnikaiḥ kriyate 
_
 yatrāpyayana pratipadyamānā vicitrābhiprāyatayā prakaraṇārthamanyathā bravate 
_
 tatrāpi vā viśeṣeṇaiva abhiprāyaviśeṣo 'numeyaḥ 
_
 vivakṣāntarād vacanāntarānutpattaḥ 
_
 abhyupagame vā sambandhavacanādapi aniścaya eva syāt kiṃ nitya tva palakṣātaḥ kṛtakatvānityatvayoḥ sambandhavacanama 
_
 uta anityatvavivakṣāta iti 
_
 
##
 atha hetutadabhāvavyavasthāyā vāstavasambandhāpekṣitvād viparītavivakṣayāpi pakatvānityatvayorastyeva sambandha iti gamakatvam 
_
 tarhi nityatvābhiprāyeṇāpi evasambandhamupadarśayataḥ tattvavāditvaṃ syāt 
_
 prakārāntareṇa sambandho sanasyavābhāvāt 
_
tathā pratijñāvacanaṃ
vinā sandigdhaviparyastāvyutpannapuruṣa pāṇā prameyaviśeṣeṣu ākāṅkṣāpratipattau vādino
viśeṣeṇa puruṣamātrasya mātrapratipādanāya pravartamānasya unmattavāditvaṃ syāta
_
 
##
 atha vivādāt puruṣaviśeṣasya prameyaviśeṣāpekṣitvapratipattiḥ 
_
 tarhi 
_
 abhyupagataiva 
_
 vivādasya tadrapatvāt 
_
 pratijñā hi pratiyogipratijñāntarama yā vivādaḥ 
_
 sādhanasahitā tu pratijñeti 
_
 na ca śāstrādeva yathokta pratipattiḥ 
_
 anamānopanyāsakāle tasyāpramāṇatvāta 
_
 prāmāṇye vā mānanati 
_
 tasmāta parārthānamānamicchatā avaśyaṃ kārya pratijñāvacanamiti 
_
 yaccedam arthādarthagatau śaktiḥ pakṣahetvabhidhānayoḥ 
_
 nārtha tena tayornāsti svataḥ sādhanasaṃsthitiḥ 
_
 ityutkam 
_
 tatra arthasyārthagatau sāmarthya na niṣidhyate 
_
 kevalayośca pakṣahetva pacānāthaparicchede sāmarthyama 
_
 avayavāntarasadabhāve ca svārthopasthāpanadvāreṇa sāmarthyamiṣyata eva 
_
 anyathā hetvabhidhānasyāpi asāmarthya parārthānumānasyāpravṛttireva 
_
 
##
 atha hetuvacanaṃ svayamasamarthamapi samarthahetusaṃsūcakatvāt parapratipattāvapahīyate 
_
 ādīyate na caivaṃ pratijñetyāha 
_
 sādhyābhidhānāta pakṣoktiḥ pāramparyeṇa nāpyalama 
_
 śaktasya sūcakaṃ hetuvaco 'śaktamapi svayam 
_
 tatra pakṣoktiḥ pratijñāvacanaṃ pāramparyeṇāpyalaṃ samarthaṃ na bhavatīti dhināṅgamiti 
_
 sādhye sādhyābhidhānamasādhāraṇameva 
_
 sapakṣāsapakṣayoraprasiddhaḥ 
_
 tathā sādhyābhidhānasya pakṣokteḥ paryāyatvāt sādhyāviśiṣṭatā ceti 
_
 atha sādhyānupayogitvāt sādhyānabhidhānam 
_
 tadapyavayavāntarasahitasya sādhya pratipādakatvādasiddham 
_
 viparyaye tu anaikāntikam 
_
 kevalasya hetuvacanasyāpi asādhakatvāt 
_
 tathā pratijñāvacanamapi asādhanāṅgamiti vadatā abhyupagatava pratijñeti vyāghātaḥ 
_
 
##
 atha svapratipattau pratijñāvacanasyānupalambhāt parapratipattāvanupādānam 
_
 evaṃ tarhi hetuvacanasyāpi adarśanādanupādānaṃ syāt 
_
 atha hetvarthasyopalambhād yuktaṃ hetuvacanam 
_
 tarhi pratijñārthasyopalabdheḥ kārya pratijñāvacanam 
_
 yathā hetvarthaḥ kāraṇaṃ sādhyapratipattau 
_
 evaṃ pratijñārthaḥ karmetyubhayoḥ kāraṇatvā viśeṣāt pakṣasyāvacane pramāṇaṃ nāstīti 
_
 upasthāpite ca karmaṇi karaṇānā pravṛtterupalambhāt tadupasthāpanārthamavaśyaṃ kārya pratijñāvacanamityalaṃ vistareṇa 
_
* avirodhigrahaṇāt
pratyakṣānumānābhyupagatasvaśāstrasvavacanavirodhino 'numeyoddeśā nirastā bhavanti * iti vyavacchedyaṃ darśayati
_
 yo hānumeyoddeśo na pratyakṣādinā virudhyate 
_
 sā pratikṣeti 
_
 
##
 anye tu pratyakṣādyaviruddho 'numeyastasyoddeśaḥ pratijñeti vyākhyāṃ kurvate 
_
 yadyapi anumeyasya sādhyasya sādhanāhatayā pratyakṣādivirodhābhāvānna vyavacchedya tva masti 
_
 tathāpi kimbhūtaṃ sādhyamityapekṣāyāṃ svarūpopavarṇanātha pratyakṣādyaviruddhapadam 
_
 pratyakṣaśabdenaiva viśiṣṭārthapratītau indriyārthasanniko dipadavaditi 
_
 taccāsat 
_
 avirodhipadasyoddeśapadena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt 
_
 karmaṇaḥ karaṇena virodhābhāvācceti 
_
 yathābhūtamupalabhyamānaṃ karma tathābhūta manupalabhyamānamapi iti uddyotakarapādairuktam 
_
 pratijñā tu karāmāta yuktastatra virodhaḥ 
_
 
##
 tatra pratyakṣavirodhī * yathā anuṣṇo 'gniḥ * iti 
_
 anu 
_
 uṣṇatāyā stvagindriyeṇa pratibhāsanāt 
_
 * dhanamambaramityanumānavirodhī * ākāśasya anumānādeva amūrtatvavibhutvaprasiddheḥ 
_
 ghanaṃ niviḍāvayavamityuddeśastena virudhyata eva 
_
 ghanatve sati asmadādīnāmasañcāraprasaṅgācceti 
_
 abhyupagata śāstravirodhī yathā * vaiśeṣikasya * sarvakāryamatpatteḥ pūrvaṃ sa dutpadyatat 
_
 iti bruvataḥ 
_
 vaiśeṣikaśāstre hi asadutpadyata iti prasiddham 
_
 * na śabdo 'rtha atyāyaka iti svavacanavirodhī 
_
 yadi hi śabdo 'rthapratyāyako na bhavati 
_
 kathamasyārthasya jñāpanārthaṃ śabdoccāraṇaṃ na virudhyeta iti 
_
 
##
 atha pramāṇatritve sati kathaṃ virodhabahutvam 
_
 lokaprasiddhayapekṣayā 
_
para āgamaviruddhasya pratyakṣaviruddhasya cāmī bhedāstathāpi svavacanaviruddhaḥ
śāstrāvaruddhaścetyādivyapadeśo janānāma atastathaivābhidhānam
_
 anamānasya tu anumānāntareṇa virodhāsambhave 'pi svakīyānamānasya balavatvādayaṃ vyapadeśo 'numānena pratijñā bādhyata iti 
_
 
##
 pratijñānantaraṃ hetulakṣaṇamāha * liṅgavacanamavadeśaḥ * iti 
_
 arthalakṣaṇatvād vacasāmiti liṅgalakṣaṇānuvāde apadeśasya mānyana prasiddham manyatrāvṛtteḥ 
_
sarvatra ceti ca vipakṣe sarvatra nāsta samakālātyayāpadiṣṭayośca vyudāsaḥ
da vacasāmiti liṅgalakṣaṇānuvādena apadeśasya lakṣaṇābhidhānamiti
_
vana sahacaritaṃ tatsamānajātīye sarvatra ca sāmānyena prasiddham * khā dhamaḥ pakṣe tatsamānaḥ sapakṣe prasiddho na pūnaviśeṣaḥ
_
 anyadharmāṇā taḥ 
_
 sarvatra ceti vyāpakāvyāpakabhedaṃ darśayati 
_
 * tadaviparīte pakṣa sarvatra nāstyeveti vipakṣādatyantavyāvṛtti darśayati 
_
 prakaraṇa tyayāpadiṣṭayośca vyudāsaḥ pūrvavadityetat * liṅgamuktam * iti diḥ 
_
 tasya vācakaṃ vacanaṃ tatīyāntaṃ paścamyantaṃ vā apadeśaḥ 
_
 ayamitarasmāt bhidyate yathoktaliṅgavacanatvāt 
_
 yastu na bhidyate tathā ca ayamitarasmāt cāsāvevam 
_
 yathā pratijñādiriti 
_
 
##
 tasya vyāpakāvyāpakasvarūpopadarśanārthama udāharaṇadvayam * yathā kriyāvattvād guṇavattvācca * iti 
_
 ca śabdena prakārāntaraṃ kriyāvatvena guṇavatvena ceti darśayati 
_
 anayorlakṣaṇenābhisambandhopadarśanārthamanuvādaḥ 
_
 tathā ca tat kriyāvattvaṃ guṇavattvañcānumeye pakṣe 'sti 
_
 tatsamānajātīye ca sapakṣe sarvasmin guṇavattvam asarvasmin kriyāvattvamastīti 
_
 * ubhayamapyetad adravye * sattādā nāstyeveti tasya guṇavattvasya kriyāvattvasya ca yathoktam 
_
 vacanamapadeśa iti siddham 
_
 
##
 * etena * sāmarthyād apadeśābhāsā nirastā bhavantīti svavākya parivarjanārthaṃ paravākye codbhāvanārthaṃ saṃlakṣyate 
_
 tatredaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇam 
_
 apadeśavadābhāsamānāḥ samyaṅ matau apadeśābhāsāḥ 
_
 aāhetravirapi va paryastabuddherhetu dā 
_
 d bhāsate iti samyaṅmatāviti padam 
_
 etasmiraṇa pakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhasya samyaṅamatau hetuvadābhāsamānatvaṃ cintyama 
_
 tasya hi para dharmatvādimatvamityato hetuvadābhāsamānatvād hetvābhāsā iti siddhaṃ lakṣaṇam 
_
 yasya tu heturapi tasya pakṣadharmatvādyapadarśanena hetṛtvapratipattau yatnaḥ kāya tpratipatterthapratipattau kāraṇatvāditi 
_
ata eva anyatarāsiddho yadyapi vṛttyā hetustathāpi pakṣadharmatayā pareṇāpratipannatvād
asiddhabuddhi janayatā pratipanne ca pramāṇataḥ pakṣadharmatvena sādhyasiddharbhāvād hetureveti
_
 
##
 anye tu ahetavaḥ pakṣadharmatvādyanyatamarūpānavidhānāt samāna hetvābhāsā iti 
_
 atha kiyatāṃ punarevamanapadeśatvamityāha * asiddhaviruddhasandigdhānadhyava sitavacanānāmanapadeśatvamuktaṃ bhavati * iti 
_
 * tatrāsiddhaścaturvidhaḥ * iti vibhāgaḥ 
_
 sāmānyalakṣaṇañca āśaṅkyamānapakṣavṛttitvam arthāllabhyate 
_
 bhāśakyamāne hi pakṣe vattiḥ sarvasya viśeṣaṇāsiddhādiprapañcasyāstīti pakṣa pāpāda sāmānyalakṣaṇam 
_
 na caivaṃ pakṣāvṛttitvaṃ tasya asamarthaviśeṣaṇādibhedeṣu asambhavāt 
_
 
##
 kena rūpeṇa caturvidha ityāha * ubhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhastadbhāvāsiddho 'numeyāsiddhaśceti 
_
 tatra * ubhayorvādiprativādinorasiddho yathā anityaḥ 
_
 sāvayavatvāditi * śabde hi sāvayavatvaṃ nityānityavādinorna prasiddha ta 
_
* anyatarāsiddho yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāditi * mīmāṃsakasya atyabhijñānādikamapalabhamānasya śabde kāryatvaṃ
tāvadasiddhaṃ yāvad anyatara sadāsadvāreṇa pramāṇato vyavasthāpyata iti niścīyate
_
 niścite dhamatve tataḥ sādhyaṃ pratipadyata eva 
_
 * tadabhāvāsiddho yathā dhamabhāvenāgyadhigato * iti 
_
 dhamatvenāniścitaṃ vāṣpādikamupalabhamānasyāgnyadhi 
_
 kartavyāyāṃ tadbhāvāsiddho dhūmabhāvasyāniścitatvāditi 
_
 * anumeyā ddhā yathā pārthivaṃ dravyaṃ tamaḥ kṛṣṇarūpatvāvattvā diti 
_
 sākhyābhyupagatasya tamaso 'prasiddhatvād ayamāśrayāsiddho na tu abhāvarūpatamo 'pekṣayā 
_
 tasya tu pramāṇena prasiddheḥ pakṣīkaraṇe kṛṣṇarūpatvaṃ 
_
 vattvaṃ 
_
 svarūpāsiddhaṃ 
_
 natvāśrayāsiddhamiti 
_
 
##
 nanvevaṃ viśeṣaṇāsiddhādiprapañcasyāsaṅagrahaṇādayukto 'yaṃ vibhāgaḥ 
_
 na 
_
 siddha'nyatarāsiddhe vā antarbhāvāt 
_
 tathā ca ubhayoviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā 
_
 śabdaḥ anabhidheyatve satibāhyendriyapratyakṣatvāt 
_
 bāhyendriyapratyakṣatve ca   anabhidheyatvāditi ubhayoviśeṣyāsiddhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtakatve sati amūrtatvāt 
_
 evamanyeṣvapi puruṣaviśeṣābhiprāyeṇa atyādhuhyamiti 
_
 asamarthaviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ prameyatve kṛtakatvāta 
_
 viparyayeṇa asamarthaviśeṣya siddha iti 
_
 vyadhikaraṇaviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ cākṣuṣatve sati kṛtakatvāt 
_
 viparyayeṇa ubhayāsiddhe 'nyatarāsiddha vā natyaḥ śabdaḥanabhidheyatve vyadhikaraṇaviśeṣyāsiddha iti 
_
 viruddhaviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatve sati amūrtatvāditi 
_
 anyathāsiddhaviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ abhyasyamānatve sati amūrtatvāditi 
_
 
##
nanvevamapi eṣāmubhayāsiddhe 'nyatarāsiddhe 'ntarbhāvavat
tadbhāvā siddhā nu meyāsiddhayorapyantarbhāvaḥ syāditi kathaṃ cāturvidhyam
_
 tayoravāntarabhedāpekṣayā tadbhāvāsiddhaḥ 
_
 parārthānumānasya prastutatvād ubhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhaśceti bhidyate 
_
 evam anumeyāsiddho 'pīti cāturvidhyam 
_
 anye tūbhayāsiddhaṃ yatra viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyañca asiddhamiti 
_
 anyatarā siddhantu viśeṣaṇāsiddhaṃ viśeṣyāsiddhaṃ veti manyante 
_
 na caitad bhāṣyakatubhi pretam 
_
 vādyabhiprāyeṇa udāharaṇopanyāsāt 
_
 anye tu svārthānumānasya tadbhāvāsiddho 'numeyāsiddhaśceti bhada sakalabhedasaṅgrāhakaḥ 
_
 parārthānumānasya tūbhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhaśceti 
_
 atra tu svārthānumānena parārthasya bhedanirūpaṇamiṣṭameva 
_
 svātantryantu niṣidhyate 
_
 
##
viruddhalakṣaṇamāha * yo hyanumeye * pakṣe vyāptyā avidyamāno 'pi tatsamā najātīye
ca sapakṣe * sarvasmin nāsti tadviparīte ca * vipakṣe 'sti *sa viparītasādhanād
viruddho yathā yasmād viṣāṇī tasmād aśva iti *
_
 viṣāṇināṃ piṇḍaṃ pakṣīkṛtya aśvo 'yam iti sādhayato viṣāṇitvād hāta hetuviruddhaḥ 
_
 asya hi anaśvenaiva vyāptatvāt 
_
 ayantu vipakṣaikadeśavṛttiḥ 
_
 vidyamānasapakṣastathā vipakṣavyāpakaḥ nitya śabdaḥ kāryatvād iti 
_
 avidyamāna sapakṣo vipakṣavyāpakaḥ sarvaṃ kārya sarvajñakartakaṃ prameyatvāditi 
_
 vidyamānasapakṣā vipakṣaikadeśavṛttiḥ 
_
 jīvaccharīraṃ sātmakaṃ kāryatvāditi 
_
 ataścatuvidhaḥ 
_
 
##
 ekasmiśca dvayorhetvoryathoktalakṣaṇayoviruddhayoḥ sannipāte sati saśayadarśanādayamanyaḥ sandigdha iti kacita 
_
 yathā mūrtatvāmūrtatvaṃ prati manasaḥ kriyāvattvāsparśavatvayoriti 
_
 nanvayamasādhāraṇa eva acākṣaṣatvapratyakṣatvavata saṃhatayoranyatarapakṣā sambhavāt 
_
 tataścānadhyavasita iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
_
 
##
 nanu śāstre tatra tatra ubhayathā darśanaṃ saṃśayakāraṇamapadiśyata iti 
_
 na 
_
 saṃśayo viṣayadvaitadarśanāta 
_
 saṃśayotpattau viṣayadvaitadarśanameva kāraṇam 
_
 tulyabalatve ca tayoḥ parasparavirodhāt nirṇayānutpādakatvaṃ syānna tu saṃśayahetutvam 
_
 na ca tayostulyabalatvamasti anyatarasyānumeyohaśasyāgamabādhitatvād ayantu viruddhabheda eva 
_
 
##
 * yastu sannanumeye * vyāptyā * tatsamānāsamānajātīyayoḥ * sapakṣa pāḥ sanneva 
_
 sa sandigdho 'naikāntikaḥ 
_
 * sandehajanakatvāt * iti kāryopanyāso na tū lakṣaṇama 
_
 indriyādiṣvapi sadabhāvenātivyāpakatvāta 
_
 jantu * yathā yasmāda viṣāṇī tasmāda gauriti viṣāṇinaṃ piṇḍa bhārati sādhayato viṣāṇitvāditi heturanaikāntikaḥ 
_
 pakṣatrayavṛtti ' ayantu sapakṣavyāpakatve sati vipakṣakadeśavṛttiḥ 
_
 agaurayaṃ viṣāṇi śata sapakṣakadeśavattitve sati vipakṣavyāpakaḥ 
_
 sapakṣavipakṣakadeśa nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavattvāta iti catavidho 'nekāntikaḥ 
_
 
##
 jaya cāturvidhyamanapapannama 
_
 anekāntikasya lakṣaṇañcāvyāpakama 
_
 viruddhā bhicāryasādhāraṇayorakhyāpanāda ityāśaṅkāpratiṣedhārtham * ekasmiśca ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 dvayorhetvovibhinnadharmisthayoḥ sannipāte saṃśayā yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāta 
_
 nityamākāśam akāryatvād iti vipakṣayoḥ sanneva 
_
 sa sa kāryopanyāso na tu lakṣaṇa pakṣīkṛtya gauriti sādhayato vi tvāt iti sapakṣakadeśavṛtti dvayoḥ * ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 hara darśanāt yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāya ekasmin dharmiṇīti padam 
_
 tathāthā na saṃśayo yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ 
_
 * yathoktalakṣaṇayoḥ * 
_
 maṇīti padam 
_
 tathāthāpyekasmin dharmiṇi dvayoḥ sannipāte 'pi yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt 
_
 nityastvamūrtakāryatvāditi tadarthaṃ 
##
 tathāpyaviruddhārthasādhakayorevaṃvidhayorapi na saṃśayahetutvaṃ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt 
_
 āśrito guṇatvāt 
_
 ato * viruddhayoḥ * viruddhārthasādhakayoḥ sannipāte saṃśayasya darśanāt * ayamanyaḥ sandigdhaḥ * anekāntika iti kecit 
_
 udāharaṇantu * yathā mūrtatvāmūrtatvaṃ prati manasaḥ kriyāvattvāsparśavattvayoriti * 
_
 mūrta manaḥ kriyāvattvāt chatravat ityekaḥ 
_
 amūrta manaḥ asparśavattvāt ākāśavat ityaparaḥ 
_
 ubhayośca pakṣadharmānvayavyatirekavattvopalabdheḥ kiṃ mūrtaṃ manaḥ syā duta amūrtamiti saṃśayaḥ 
_
 
##
 tadasat 
_
 abhayoḥ prayogāsambhavāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 ekasmin sādhane prayukta tasya nirduṣṭatāyāṃ sādhyasiddharanyasya upanyāsānupapattiḥ 
_
 duṣṭatāyāṃ vā saiva asya abhidheyeti 
_
 na ca parasparaviruddhārthasādhakatvameva anumānayordoṣaḥ 
_
 pramā gena ubhayorekatra sadbhāvasiddhau virodhasyābhāvaprasaṅgāt 
_
 avyabhicāryānumā nayośca avaśyamarthavyavasthāpakatvam 
_
 avyabhicārasya tallakṣaṇatvāt 
_
 viparyaye tu vyabhicāritvameva 
_
 yathā mūrtaṃ mano 'sparśavattve sati kriyāvattvāt 
_
 amūrtañca kriyāvattve satyasparśavattvāt iti samastayoḥ prayogaḥ 
_
 
##
 tatrāpi asādhāraṇamityāha * nanvayamasādhāraṇa eva acākṣuṣatvapratyakṣa tvavat 
_
 saṃhatayoranyatarapakṣāsambhavāt * iti 
_
 yathā hi 
_
rūpātīndriyaguṇavyati rekeṇa anyaguṇānāṃ guṇavyavahāre sādhyasāmānyavattvād
dravyatve sati niyamenācā kṣuṣatvaṃ heturna sapakṣe rūpādāvasti
_
 nāpi vipakṣe ghaṭādāvityasādhāraṇaḥ 
_
tadvat sahacarayoḥ kriyāvattvāsparśavattvayoranyatarapakṣāsambhavādityanyatarasmin sapakṣe vipakṣe vā asambhavād asādhāraṇatvam
_
 na cāsyāsaṅgraha ityāha * tataścānadhyavasita iti vakṣyāmaḥ * 
_
 
##
 yad vā cākṣuṣatvapratyakṣatvavat iti vaidhodāharaṇam 
_
 yathā hi guṇaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānyavattvād dravyatve sati niyamena acākṣuṣapratyakṣatvāt andhādiva diti 
_
asya sapakṣakadeśe vartamānasya vipakṣādatyantaṃ vyāvṛttirna caivaṃ
kriyāva ttvāsparśavattvayorityāha * saṃhatayoranyatarapakṣāsambhavāt * iti
_
 
##
evaṃ viruddhāvyabhicāriṇo 'sādhāraṇasyacasaṃśayahetutve nirākṛte
sūtravirodha mudbhāvayannāha * nanuśāstretatra tatrobhayathā darśanaṃ
saṃśayakāraṇamapadiśyate * iti tatra tatra śāstre tasmistasmin sūtre dṛṣṭañca dṛṣṭavat dṛṣṭaca manasi mānābhisambaddha ubhayacā
_
 parāyā bhavati 
_
 dṛṣṭañca manasi kriyāvatvaṃ punardaṣṭena tulyaṃ vartata iti sad asparśavattvam 
_
 ato viruddhasādhanābhisambaddhaṃ mano dṛṣṭvā saṃśete ki mūtam uta amūrta mana iti 
_
 'yathā dṛṣṭam ayathādṛṣṭañca ' saṃśaya ityasādhāraṇasya ca saṃśayahetutvamuktam 
_
 yathā dṛṣṭaṃ pakṣe 
_
 dṛṣṭa sapakṣe 
_
 vipakṣe ca na dṛṣṭama 
_
 ata ubhayathā dṛṣṭatvāt 
##
yad vā yathādṛṣṭaṃ kriyāvattvena punarayathādṛṣṭam aspara ' ubhābhyāṃ saha dṛṣṭatvāt saṃśaya ityuktaṃ paraṇāha 
_
 viṣayadvaitadarśanādutpatteḥ 
_
 asyaiva vivaraṇam * saṃśayotpattau viṣa nameva kāraṇam * iti 
_
 viṣayadvaite dṛśyata iti viṣayadvaitadarśanaṃ sāmā yasya vā dvaitaṃ vaividhyaṃ yasya 
_
 tat tathoktaṃ sāmānyaṃ tadarśanameva 
_
 paśaṣānuvṛttihetutvāta saṃśayakāraṇaṃ na viruddhahetusannipātaḥ 
_
 
##
asādhāraṇa ' viruddhaviśeṣaiḥ sahānapalambhena tasya tatsmārakatvānupapatteḥ 
_
manusmṛtihetuśca dharmaḥ saṃśayakāraṇaṃ
na parasparavirodhī samānabala mānabalatve ca * tayoḥ paraspara virodhāta itarasyetareṇa pratibandhāta utpādakatvaṃ
syānna saṃśayahetutvam * tailādinābhyaktasya śāli   svāṅakurānatpādakatvavaditi abhyupagamyaitadaktam
_
 paramārthato jyāstulyabalatvamasti * anyatarasya amūrta mana iti * anumeyodde parādhitvāt * iti 
_
 tathā cāgamaḥ tadabhāvādaṇu manaḥ' saṃśayasya viṣayadvaitadarśanādura yadvaitadarśanameva kāraṇam nyameva 
_
 viṣayasya vā dvara viruddhaviśeṣānuvṛttihata dharmo vā 
_
 viruddhāva viruddhaviśeṣānusmṛtiharu iti 
_
 samānabalatva * nirṇayānutpādakatvaṃ syānna bījasya svāṅakura * na ca tayostulyabala śasyāgamavirodhitvāt * iti 
_
 mūrtatvañca avyāpita vacanamapramāṇam 
_
 tarhi manaḥ sadbhāvāsiddharāśrayāsiddhamanumāna māṇam 
_
 tarhi ma bhūtatvānabhyupagame māvana yugapaj
##
 athedaṃ vacanamapramāṇam 
_
 tarhi manaḥ 
_
 miti yathoktalakṣaṇānupapattiḥ 
_
 na ca tyāpi manaḥsadbhāvasiddhiḥ 
_
 jñānotpattiprasaṅgāta 
_
 ataḥ pratijñā na yathoktalakṣaṇamiti 
_
 viruddhād bhidyate iti vi panyāsāt 
_
 sadbhāvasiddhiḥ 
_
 amartasya sakalendriyādhiṣṭhāyakatvena yagapaja 
_
 māt 
_
 ataḥ pratijñāvacanasyāgamena virodhād amūrtānumānaṃ kṣaṇāmati 
_
 ayantu viruddhabhedaḥ pratijñāvasare 'bhihita eva 
_
 bhidyate iti viruddhabhedaḥ kālātyayāpadiṣṭaḥ 
_
 duṣṭapakṣopanyāsānantaramu 
##
 sūtradvitayañca ekadharmiviṣayatvena saṃśayapratipādanārthamiti vyākhyeyam 
_
 tathā ca 
_
 niyatasāmānyavastu pratiniyataviśeṣaiḥ sahacaritamekadā dṛṣṭaṃ punasta ttulyam anyaviśeṣāvinābhūtam 
_
 ataḥ kālāntare deśavyavadhānavaśāt tad dṛṣṭvā saṃśete kimidamevam āhosvidevaṃ na bhavatīti 
_
 tathā ekadharmi viṣayatve 'pi 
_
 yathādṛṣṭam iti kiñcit sāmānyavadvastu kenacid viśeṣeṇa saha dṛṣṭam 
_
 ayathādṛṣṭam tadevopalabdhiviśeṣaśūnyaṃ viśeṣāntarasahitaṃ dṛṣṭam 
_
 ata ubhayathā dṛṣṭatvādubhābhyāṃ saha dṛṣṭatvād ubhayaśūnyasyopalabdhau tatsmaraṇa tu asati 
_
 saṃśayo bhavatīti 
_
 yathā devadattaṃ sakeśamupalabhya punarniṣkeśam 
_
 ataḥ kālāntare tameva veṣṭitaśirasamupalabhamānasya kimayaṃ sakeśo niṣkeśo veti saṃśayo bhavatīti 
_
 
##
 samastasapakṣe tu asādhāraṇasyānadhyavasitvamāha * yaśca sannanumaya tatsamānāsamānajātīyayoḥ * sapakṣavipakṣayoḥ 
_
 asanneva so 'nyatarā siddho 'nadhyavasāyahetutvāt * niścayānupādakatvāt 
_
 atastaddhetutvād * ana dhyavasitaḥ * 
_
 * yathā sat kāryam utpatteḥ ityudāharaṇam 
_
 sakala kāya mutpatteḥ prāk sadanu 
_
 dutpadyamānatvāditi hetarna pratyā 
_
 ākāśādā nāpi kharaviṣāṇādāvityanadhyavasitaḥ 
##
na cāsya sūtreṇāsaṅgraha ityāha * ayamaprasiddho 'napadeśaḥ iti vacanādavaruddhaḥ * sapakṣavipakṣayoraprasiddhatvāditi

 evamasādhāraṇasya saśayahetutve niraste satravirodhamadabhāvayannāha nanu cāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ saṃśaya māhataḥ śāstre 
_
 talyajātīyeṣu * sapakṣeṣu 
_
 * arthāntarabhūteṣu vipakṣaṣu 
_

_
 * viśeṣasya * asādhāraṇadharmasya 
_
 * ubhayathā 
_
 * sapakṣe vipakṣe ca daṣṭatvāta iti 
_
 anenāsādhāraṇasya saśaya samityāṅakyāha * na * 
_
 sūtrasya 
_
 anyārthatvāta  sattāsambandhi 
_
 athaśabdavācyatvācca kiṃ dravyaṃ gaṇaḥ karma vā śabda iti saṃśayaḥ 
_
 na sambandhāt 
_
 śrāvaṇatvācca *ityakte* sūtrakāreṇa 
_
 paro brūte viśeṣasyopalabdhaḥ kathaṃ śabde saṃśaya ityāśaṅakyāha * masya* iti 
_
 na dravyasya gaṇasya karmaṇo vā viśeṣaḥ śrāvaṇatvam 
_
 sāmānyameva sampadyate 
_
 kasmāta

##
* yasmāta guṇatve śabdasya sādhye sāyaṣu* rūpādiṣa śaklatvādiviśeṣo guṇatvena sahacarito dṛṣṭaḥ 
_
 paraṃ sattāsambandhāt 
_
 nāmanyatamasya * iti 
_
*tulyajātīyeṣu * rūpādiṣu * arthāntarabhūteṣa * utkṣepaṇādiṣu viśeṣo dṛṣṭastathā pṛtha bhedānām
* draya dṛṣṭatvāt dravyatvaguṇa śrāvaṇatvaṃ viśeṣastad dravyatvādivi sato 'yaṃ viśeṣaḥ śrāvaṇatvam
_
 guṇasya kāraṇaṃ śrāvaṇatvam 
_
 na tu asa dhāraṇadharmopalabdhau * sa saṃśayakāraṇatvam anvayavyā na ca sarvasmād vyāvṛtta bhāvāt saṃśayo yuktaḥ

##
sadbhāva bhāvāt 
_
 * tasmāt sāmāna bhūtaṣu * utkṣepaṇādiṣu karmatvena sahacarita utkṣepaṇatvādi dṛṣṭastathā pṛthivyādiṣu pṛthivītvādivyatveneti 
_
 * dravyādi * dravyagaṇakarmaṇāma 
_
 * ekaikaśaḥ * pratyekam 
_
 * kaikaśaḥ pratyekama 
_
 viśeṣasyobhayathā vara * dravyatvaguṇatvādisahacaritasya dṛṣṭatvāt 
_
 upalabhyate ca śabde viśaṣastad dravyatvādiviṣayaṃ smaraṇaṃ bhavatyeva 
_
 ataḥ kiṃ dravyasya paḥ śrāvaṇatvam 
_
 guṇasya karmaṇo vā 
_
 ityuktena nyāyena saṃśaya ṇatvam 
_
 na tu asādhāraṇatvena 
_
 * ṣaṭsvapi padārtheṣu * asā palabdhau * saṃśayaprasaṃṅgāt * 
_
 utkṣepaṇatvādiviśeṣānupalabdheśca svam anvayavyatirekābhyāmupalabdham na tadupalabdheḥ

##
 na ca sarvasmād vyāvattaṃ viśeṣamupalabhamānasya viruddhaviśeṣānasmatera sayā yuktaḥ 
_
 sadabhāve 'pyanucchedaḥ syāta 
_
 nirṇayotpattikāraṇā tasmāt sāmānyapratyakṣādeva saṃśayaḥ * na viśeṣadarśanādityupasaṃhāraḥ 
_
 yad vā viśeṣavattvasyobhayathā sapakṣavipakṣāviśeṣitasyopalabdhestadūpalambhā saṃśayaḥ 
_
 na saṃśayakāraṇam asādhāraṇo dharmaḥ 
_
 ṣaṭsvapi padārtheṣu saṃśayaprasaṅgāditi 
_
 śeṣaṃ pūrvavat

##
 athāpadeśānantaraṃ nidarśanasvarūpanirūpaṇārtham * dvividhaṃ nidarśanam * ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 dvividhamiti vibhāgo nidarśanamiti niruktilakṣaṇam 
_
 nidarśyate sādhyasādhanayorbahivyāptirasmin iti nidarśanaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
_
 tathā nidarśāte sādhyasādhanayorvyāptiraneneti nidarśanaṃ vyāptipratipādakaṃ dṛṣṭānta vacanam

 tathāhi

_
 yastu na bhidyate na cāsāvevaṃ yathā pratijñādiriti

##
 tat kena rūpeṇa dvividham 
_
 * sādharmyaṇa vaidhayeṇa ca * iti 
_
 * tatrā numeyasāmānyena * sādhyasāmānyena 
_
 * liṅgasāmānyasya * sādhanasāmānyasya 
_
 * anuvidhānadarśana sādharmyanidarśanam * 
_
 sādhanasāmānyaṃ vyāpyam 
_
 vyāpaka ca sādhyasāmānyamiti 
_
 * yad yat kriyāvat tattad dravyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yathā śaraḥ * ityudāharaṇam 
_
 atra hi dravyatvavyāptau kriyāvattvaṃ sādhanamastīti 
_
 * anumeyaviparyaye * sādhyaviparyaye 
_
 * liṅgasya * sādhanasya 
_
 * abhāvadaśana vaidharmyanidarśanam tadyathā yad yad adravyaṃ tat tat kriyāvanna bhavati

##
 * anena nidarśanābhāsāḥ nidarśanavadābhāsanta iti nidarśanābhā satsamānadharmāṇaḥ 
_
 * nirastā bhavanti   iti svavākye parivarjanārthaṃ para cādbhāvanārthaṃ nirūpyante 
_
 tad yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amṛtatvāta 
_
 yad amūrta dṛṣṭaṃ tannityaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ 
_
 yathā paramāṇuḥ * iti 
_
 sādhanasyā tya paramāṇāvabhāvāta sādhanavikalamudāharaṇam 
_
 asminneva sādhye kamāta' sādhyavikalam 
_
 nityatvasya karmaṇyabhāvāt 
_
 yathā sthālo sāpakalam 
_
 nityatvasyāmūrtatvasya ca sthālyāmabhāvāt 
_
 yathā tamaḥ māsiddham 
_
 sāṃkhyābhyupagatasya tamasoprasiddhatvāt 
_
 ambaravat iti sāvyasādhanādhikaraṇatve 'pi ani nagato vacanadoṣaḥ 
_
 yad yad amūrta dṛṣṭaṃ natya dṛṣṭaṃ yathā ambaramiti vacanaṃ vinā anugatasyāpratīteḥ

##
yad vā samyagdṛṣṭānto 'pi ākāśāsattvavādino na sādhyasiddhi karāti
yāvanna pramāṇato vyavasthāpyata ityābhāsa ucyā tājñāpanārtham
_
 itthambhūta iti 
_
 anye tu ābhāsāvasare samyagadṛṣṭāntopadarśanam ābhāsānām ābhāsa m 
_
 itthambhūtaṃ hi nidarśanam 
_
 etatpratirūpakāṇi ca tadābhāsā tathā vyāpyavyāpakabhāvapratipatti dravyatvopalabdheḥ 
_
 samavyāptike 'pi pattirna syāditidūṣaṇa 
##
 yad yad dravyaṃ tattat kriyāvad dṛṣṭam * iti ca vipa atā dravyatvaṃ vyāpyaṃ kiyāvattvañca vyāpakaṃ syādāta * māvapratipattiḥ 
_
 na caitadasti 
_
 ākāśādau kriyāvattvaṃ vināpi yaḥ 
_
 samavyāpti ke 'pi sādhanasya vyāpakatvābhidhāne sādhyasya prati dātadūṣaṇam 
_
 viṣamavyāptike viparītānugamo doṣo na samavyāptike 
_
 atropasaṃhāravākyaṃ liñca 
_
 anameyaśca 
_
 ubhayañca 
_
 āśrayaśceti pāśrayāḥ 
_
 te asiddhā yeṣu ābhāseṣu te tathoktāḥ 
_
 te ca ananu rātānugatāśceti * liṅgānumeyobhayāśrayāsiddhānanugataviparītāna iti cānye

##
vaidharmyanidarśanābhāsān darśayati * yadanityaṃ tanmūrtaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yathā karma * iti sādhanāvyāvṛttam 
_
 tasya hi amūrtatvāditi 
_
 tasminneva sādhye yathā paramāṇuḥ iti sādhyāvyāvṛttaṃ vyatirekodāharaṇam 
_
 paramāṇonityatvāditi 
_
 yathā ākāśam ityubhayāvyāvṛttam 
_
 amūrtatvasya nityatvasya ca tatrāvyāvṛtti riti 
_
 yathā tamaḥ iti dharmāsiddham 
_
 sāṃkhyābhyupagatasya tamaso 'prasiddhatvā diti 
_
 ghaṭavat ityubhayāvyāvṛttāvapi avyatirekaḥ 
_
 yad yannityaṃ na bhavati tattadamṛtaṃ na bhavatīti vacanaṃ vinā vyatirekasyāpratipatteḥ 
_
 ghaṭāsattvavādino vā pramāṇenāpratipādito na sādhyasiddhi karotīti ābhāsa ucyate

##
* yanniṣkriyaṃ tad adravyaṃ dṛṣṭam * iti vyatirekaḥ 
_
 sādhyavyāvṛttyā hi sādhana vyāvṛttirvācyā 
_
 na tu sādhanavyāvṛttyā sādhyavyāvṛttiḥ 
_
 kriyāvattvābhāve 'pi ākāśādau dravyatvasya sādhyasyāvyāvṛtteḥ 
_
 sādhanābhāvo hi vyāpakaḥ sādhyā bhāvo vyāpya iti 
_
 eteṣāmupasaṃhāraḥ 
_
 liṅgacca 
_
 anumeyaśca 
_
 ubhayañceti liṅgānumeyobhayāni

##
 evaṃ saha ābhāsainidarśanamupadarthya anusandhānanirūpaṇārthamāha * nidarśane 'numeyasāmānyena saha * ityādi

 * nidarśane * dṛṣṭānte 
_
 * anumeyasāmānyena * sādhyasāmānyena 
_
 * saha dṛṣṭasya liṅgasāmānyasya anumeye * pakṣe 
_
 * anvānayana manusandhānam * 
_
 ānayanaṃ pratipādanamanyasyāpi sambhavatīti liṅgasyeti padam 
_
 tathāpi liṅgasya nidarśane pratipādanamastīti tadvyudāsāya anumeyapadam

anumeye ca gṛhītāvinābhāvasya liṅgasya pratipādakaṃ
hetuvacanamapīti nidarśane'numeyasāmānyena saha dṛṣṭasya liṅgasāmānyasyeti padam

##
 saṅgrahoktevivaraṇamāha * anumeyadharmamātratvenābhihitaṃ liṅgasāmānyam * na tu samarthamiti mātrābhidhānena darśayati

 * anupalabdhaśaktikam * iti

 punaḥ * nidarśane 'numeya dharmasāmānyena saha dṛṣṭam *

##
 tadapi dvividham 
_
 sādharmyaṇa vaidharyeṇa ca 
_
 tatra anumeyasāmānyena saha liṅgasāmānyasya nidarśane sattvamupalabhyābhisandhatte tathā cāyaṃ kriyāvān vāyu riti 
_
vaidharmyanidarśane tu anumeyasya dravyatvasyābhāve ca tasya
kriyāvattvasyā sattvamupalabhya na ca tathā vāyuniṣkriya ityupasaṃhāraḥ
_
 niṣkriyatvapratiṣedhena kriyāvattvamupasaṃharatīti 
_
 pṛthagvacanantu pratiṣedhābhiprāyeṇaiva

##
 nanu vyarthamanusandhānavacanam 
_
 tadantareṇāpi hetuvacanād gṛhītavyāptikāt sādhyasiddheḥ 
_
 na 
_
 anena vinā abādhitaviṣayatvasyāpratipatteḥ 
_
 hetuvacanantu kāraṇamātropasthāpakam 
_
 na tu gṛhītavyāptikasya antarvyāptipratipādaka miti 
_
 yathābhūtena dravyatvāvinābhāvinā pramāṇāntarāviruddhena kriyāvattvena kriyāvān karaḥ 
_
 tathā ca vāyurityantāptipratipattiḥ 
_
 tadabhāve tu bahirvyāpti sadbhāve 'pi na gamakatvam 
_
 yathā śabdasya anityatve sādhye sāmānyavattve sati cākṣuṣapratyakṣaḥ 
_
 tasya kālātyayāpadiṣṭa sya 
_
 tvaṃ ceti 
_
 ata evātropanayavacanaṃ na nirviṣayatvādapramāṇam

##
 na copasaṃhāra vinā dharmiviśeṣeṇa sambandhāprasiddhau tatraiva sādhyaviśeṣa pratipattiḥ syāt 
_
 svārthānumānakāle ca upanayārthasyopalabdheḥ kārya tad vacanam 
_
 svapratipattyanusāreṇa parārthānumānapravṛtteḥ 
_
 na ca svapratipattāvetasyā satvam 
_
 avinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇānantaraṃ parāmaśaṃjñānasyānubhavāt 
_
 anabhyu pagame ca sambandhasmaraṇasyāniyatatvāt niyatapradeśe pratipattirna syādityuktam

##
 tasmād ayamityaparokṣatānirdeśasyāvinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇānantara mupalabdharasti parāmarśajñānam 
_
 atastadupanyāsārtha kāryamanusandhānavacanamiti 
_
 atha pratyāmnāyasvarūpopadarśanārtham * anumeyatvenoddiṣṭe * ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 * anumeyatvena * anumānayogyatvena 
_
 * uddiṣṭe cāniścite ca pareṣām * saṃśayitaviparyastāvyutpannānām 
_
 punaḥ * niścayāpādanārthaṃ pratijñāyāḥ punaḥ vacanaṃ pratyāmnāyaḥ

##
 saṅgrahoktevivaraṇamāha anumeye dharmamātre * pratipādyatvena * sādhyatvena 
_
 * uddiṣṭe cāniścite ca pareṣām * 
_
 kiṃ viśiṣṭānām 
_
 * hetvādibhira 
_
 vayavairā hitaśaktīnām * iti 
_
 āhitā śaktiravinābhāvo yasya liṅgasya yastaistathoktaisteṣām 
_
 etasmāt sādhanād bhaviṣyati sādhyasiddhirityava kṛtāsthānāmiti bhāvaḥ 
_
 * niścayāpādanārthaṃ pratijñāyāḥ punarvacana pratyāmnāyaḥ * iti 
_
 punaruktamātravyavacchedārtha pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanamiti padam 
_
 tathāpi anityaḥ śabdo 'nityaḥ śabda iti punaruktavyu dāsārthaṃ niścayā pādanārthamiti padam 
_
 avipratipannasya etasmādapi niścayo bhavatīti tadaya pareṣāmiti 
_
tathāpi teṣāṃ madhye kasyacid
ekāvayavopadarśanena anvayavyātara kānusmaraṇadvāreṇa arthapratipattirbhavatīti * parisamāptena vākyena * iti grahaṇam

 yasminnavayave sati vākyaṃ parisamāpyata iti

 tadevaṃ pratyāmnāya

##
 nanu pratijñāvacanasya tu vināśitvena avasthānāsambhavāt kathaṃ punarvacana miti 
_
 tatsamānaśabdoccāraṇāt

yathā kṣaṇikatve 'pi karmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ samānāmi nayakaraṇāt punarnṛtyatīti vyapadeśastadvat
pratijñāsamāna śabdaprayogakaraṇāra punarvacanabhiti vyapadeśo bhavatyeva
_
 atiśaye pūnaḥśabdo vivakṣita 
_
 pratijñā pakṣastasya punarvacanaṃ ghaṭata eva

##
 liṅgavākyārthavādinastu pratijñāyate 'neneti pratijñā liṅgaṃ tasya punarvacanaṃ pratyāmnāya iti 
_
 udāharaṇantu * tasmād dravyameveti * 
_
 etena adravyatvapratipādaka pramāṇābhāvo 'pyupadarśita eva

 taduktam

##
 'ḍiṇḍikarāgaṃ parityajyākṣiṇī nimīlya cintaya tāvat ki iyatārtha māttabhavati naveti

 yadi iha bhavati kimanayā śabdamālayā 
_
 na bhavatīti   vācyaṃ dṛṣṭatvāt' natadevaṃ

##
 atha pratijñāderevārthapratipādakatvamastu 
_
 ki pratyāmnāyena 
_
 tathāhi 
_
pratijñāvacanaiviṣayavyavasthāpanād hetūdāharaṇābhyāṃ
vahirvyāptiprasiddhau upanaya nāntaryāptyupadarśane sati avaśyamabhipretārthasiddhiriti
_
 satyametata 
_
 tathāpi avaśyambhāvino 'rthasya pratijñādinā pratipāditasya pratipādanārthamavaśyaṃ kāya nigamanamityāha * na hyetasmin * iti 
_
 na pūrveṣāmavayavānāṃ samastānā tadarthavācakatvamasti 
_
vyastānāmitaretaravyāvṛttasvārthavyavasthāpane caritāya tvamityanyadato vācyaṃ

##
 atha sādhanasya antarvyāptibahirvyāptyabhidhāne sati sādhyaviśeṣo gamya evetyāha * gamyamānārthatvāditi cenna 
_
 atiprasaṅgāta 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 pratijñāna hetumātrābhidhānaṃ kartavyam * svata eva viduṣāṃ hetūpalambhe sati anvayamā rekānusmaraṇaṃ 
_
 tasmāccādhigatirbhaviṣyatīti viśeṣābhidhānavaiyayaṃ syāt 
_
 
##
 atha paraṃ pratipādayatā vacanenaiva pratipādana kāryamiti śeṣāṇā prayā hi vākyārthapratipādanārthaṃ nigamanamapi kāryama 
_
 na ca pratipādyāmitrā prayogo yuktaḥ 
_
 tasya manuṣyadharmaṇā sākṣādapratīteravyavasthāpanācca 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 kāścadekasmādeva avayavādarthaṃ pratipadyate 
_
 kaścid dvābhyām 
_
 anyastribhiritya navasthitatvāt pratipādyānāṃ tadabhiprāyāniścaye prayogānupapattireva syāt 
_
 ataḥ paraṃ pratipādayatā svapratipattyupāyopadarśanaṃ kāryamiti pañcānāṃ prayogo purataḥ 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 pradeśasthaṃ dhamamupalabhya avinābhāvasambandhaṃ smṛtvā tathā pāya dhūmavāniti parāmṛśati 
_
tataḥ sādhyaṃ pratipadyate tasmādagnimāniti jagamanārthasyāpyupalabdheḥ parapratipādanāya tadupanyāso yukta eveti pañcānāṃ
bhāgaḥ kārya ityāha bhāṣyakāraḥ tasmādatraivārthaparisamāptiḥ iti
_
 
##
 anye tu antarvyāptipratipādanārthaṃ nigamanamiti manyante 
_
 anusandhānāt vyāpakatvaprasiddhau viparītaprasaṅgapratiṣedhārthaṃ nigamanamiti 
_
 viparītārthavyavasthāpakapramāṇasyāprāmāṇyopadarśane sati pakṣe vyāptiḥ cāyata eva 
_
 yatra ca parapakṣāpratiṣedhastatra hetonaṃ gamakatvam 
_
 yathā mūryo 'tatputratvāt upalabhyamānatatputravaditi 
_
 atra hi tatputrasya amūrkhatve na cad bādhakamastīti tatsādhakapramāṇābhāvaśca niścita eveti anyathāsiddhaṃ sādhanametat 
_
 
##
 athāvinābhūtasya pramāṇavirodhābhāvāna yuktaṃ viparītapramāṇasyāprāmā padaśanamiti cenna 
_
 tadantareṇāvinābhāvasyaivāprasiddheḥ 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 nityatva pādakapramāṇasya prāmāṇye sati na śabde kṛtakatvasyānityatvena vyāptiḥ yādāta 
_
 na ca parapakṣapratiṣedhakādeva svapakṣasiddhiḥ 
_
 vyadhikaraṇatvāt 
_
 vārāpa vaiyarthyaprasaṅgācceti 
_
 parapakṣapratiṣedhe tūpadarśitabahirvyāptikaṃ pakṣe palabhyamānaṃ bhavatyeva sādhanamiti nigamanaprayogaḥ kāryaḥ 
_
 
##
 atha pratijñāvacanameva parapakṣapratiṣedhasahāyaṃ sādhanamiti cenna 
_
 tasya mātrābhidhāyakatvāta 
_
 sādhyama iti arhatyarthe 
_
 śakyārthe vā kṛtya 
_
 tābhi katha tadvacanāt tasya siddhiḥ 
_
 tasmād bahirvyāptivadantāpti samarthayatā taviṣayatvāsatpratipakṣatvapratipādanārthameva avayavāntaramabhidheyam

##
 atha prakaraṇasamakālātyāpadiṣṭayorapi bahirvyāptisabhāvāt gamakatvaṃ 
_
 bhasti ca tayoḥ pakṣavyāpakatve satyanvayavyatirekasadbhāva iti 
_
 ayuktametat 
_
 tādātmyatadutpattilakṣaṇapratibandhāyattastu avyabhicāro na bhavatī tyuktaṃ vyāptisamarthanāvasare 
_
 tasmāduktanyāyena atraivārthaparisamāptiriti

##
evaṃ vibhinnaprakaraṇeṣu avayavānāṃ svarūpopadarśane 'pi ekatra tatsvarūpa parijñānāpekṣayā praśnaḥ * katham * iti 
_
 * anityaḥ śabda ityanana aniścitānityatvamātraviśiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ kathyate * iti pratijñaiṣā 
_
 * prayatnā nantarīyakatvādityanena anityatvasādhanadharmamātramabhidhīyate * na tu samarthamiti hetuvacanam 
_
* iha yat prayatnānantarīyakaṃ tadanityaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ
yathā ghaṭa ityanena sādhyasāmānyena sādhanasāmānyasyānugamamātramucyate * hāta sādharyodāharaṇam
_
 * nityam aprayatnānantarīyakaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yathā ākāśam ityanena sādhyābhāvena saha sādhanasyāsattvaṃ vyākhyāyate 
_
 
##
pradaśyate * śata vaidharyodāharaṇam 
_
 * tathā ca prayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ * na ca tathā prayatnā nantarīyako na bhavatīti 
_
 * anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ dṛṣṭasāmarthyasya sādhanasāmānya sya śabde 'nusandhāna gamyate 
_
 tasmādanityaḥ eva 
_
 śabdaḥ ityanana anitya eva śabda iti pratipipādayiṣitārthaparisamāptirgamyate* ityabhipretātha siddhirbhavatīti 
_
 ataḥ * pañcāvayavenaiva vākyena pareṣāṃ svaniścitārthaprati pādanaṃ kriyate iti siddham 
_
 atra ca śabdaviśeṣasya pakṣīkaraṇe prayatnānantarīyakatvaṃ sādhanaṃ vivakṣita miti jñeyam 
_
 anyathā hi śabdamātraparigrahe prayatnānantarīyakatvaṃ bhāgāsincha syāt 
_
 na hi prayatnānantaraṃ sarvaśabdānāṃ janmāstīti 
_
 
##
 atha nirṇayo vidyāntaramiti kecit 
_
 taniṣedhārthaṃ * viśeṣadarśanajam   ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 parārthānumānānantaramasyāntarbhāvanirūpaṇamatrāpi antarbhāva śāpanārtham 
_
 nirṇaya iti lakṣyanirdeśo 'vaśiṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇam 
_
 avadhāraṇajñānaṃ hi viṣayayajñānamapi bhavati na tu viśeṣadarśanājjāyate 
_
 viśeṣadarśanajaṃ cobha 
_
 ca saṃśa yajñānamapītyavadhāraṇagrahaṇam

##
 tathāpi viśeṣadarśanajamavadhāraṇajñānaṃ nirṇaya ityukte vyabhicārābhāvād saṃśayavirodhīti padam 
_
 na 
_
 viśiṣṭanirṇayalakṣaṇārthatvāt 
_
yadyapi padarśanajamavadhāraṇajñānamiti sakalanirṇayavyāpīdaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ
tathāpi virodhīti padaṃ saṃśayapūrvakasya nirṇayasya lakṣaṇārtham
_
 tathā ca naiyāyikai vimṛśya pakṣapratipakṣābhyāmarthāvadhāraṇaṃ nirṇayaḥ' taśayapūrvakasya lakṣaṇam 
_
 vimṛśyeti vimarśa kṛtvā 
_
 pakṣapratipakṣābhyāmiti nābhyām 
_
 sa punaḥ sādhanadūṣaṇābhyāṃ nirṇaya iti

##
 atha viśeṣadarśanāt saṃśayo vyāvartate

 na nirṇayāditi kathaṃ tadvirodhitvam 
_
 upacāreṇa 
_
 nirṇayakāraṇasya saṃśayavirodhitvāt nirṇayastavirodhītyuktam

 asyāntarbhāvamāha * etadeva pratyakṣamanumānaṃ vā * na jñānāntaram 
_
 sāmagnījanyaṃ hi pratyakṣamanumānasāmagrījanyantu anumānamiti 
_
 * yad daśanāt saṃśayavirodhyutpadyate sa nirṇayaḥ * iti prāktanasya vivaraṇam 
_
 viśeṣadarśanāt saṃśayā 
##
atra * sthāṇupuruṣayorūlatāmātrasādṛśyālocanād viśeṣaṣvapratyakṣeṣūbhaya pānusmaraṇāt   kimayaṃ
sthāṇuḥ puruṣo veti saṃśayotpattau satyāṃ śiraḥ pāṇyādiviśeṣadarśanāt puruṣa evāyamityavadhāraṇajñānam indriyārthasannikarṣā ta

 pratyakṣanirṇayaḥ

##
 atha smṛteḥ kāryakāraṇaviṣayasvarūpanirūpaṇārthaṃ *liṅgadarśanecchānu

##
 anye tu dṛṣṭaścakṣuṣā 
_
 anubhūtastvagindriyeṇeti

 tatra liṅgaṃ darśayati * śeṣānuvyavasāyānusmaraṇecchādveṣahetuḥ * iti

 tasya heturavinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇam 
_
 tathā padasmaraṇā vākyasmaraṇam 
_
 sukhasmaraṇādiccho duḥkhasmaraṇāda dveṣa iti

##
 atha codanaiva bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyantaṃ viprakṛṣṭādikamarthaṃ prakāśayati nātha kiñcana indriyādikamiti cenna 
_
 anamānasyāpi atītādyarthaprakāśana palambhāt 
_
 tathā ca 
_
 meghonnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭirityanumīyate 
_
 nadāpūra viśiṣṭād upariṣṭād vṛṣṭirityuktam

 pratyakṣañcātra avinābhāvagrāhaka yam

 anyathā vyāptigrahaṇābhāve 'numānameva na pravarteta

 na cānumānanā bhāvagrahaṇam 
_
 anavasthāprasaṅgāt

 vartamānena cāvinābhāvagrahaṇe katham atītādyarthānumānaṃ syāt

##
 anye tu atīto vyavahito viṣayo yasyānubhavasyāsau atītaviṣayaḥ 
_
 saviṣayo yasyāḥ sā atītaviṣayeti prāpte sati ekasya viṣayasya lopo draṣṭavya ityatītānubhavaviṣayatvaṃ labhyata iti manyante 
_
 atha arthajatvameva smateḥ kasmānneṣyate 
_
 arthavināśe 'pyutpādāt 
_
 yaddaśakālāliṅgite 'nabhavajñānamatpannaṃ tadālambanameva nyāyyam 
_
 smṛtikāle tasyāvidyamānatayā viṣayatvābhāvāt 
_
 bāhyendriyāṇāñca smṛtijanmani vyābhacārādantaḥkaraṇasya vyāpāro niścīyate 
_
 na ca tasya svātantryeṇa bāhaviṣaye vyāpāraḥ sambhavatīti anarthajatvameva nyāyyam 
_
 avaśyañca yatva sati avyabhicāritvādidharmopetatvāt pramārūpatāyāṃ smṛteḥ pramāṇā uttavācyā 
_
 anamānādeśca vyāpārānupalabdherantaḥkaraṇasya svātantryeṇa uttiā prāmāṇye sati smateraparokṣatvaṃ syāta 
_
 na caitadasti 
_
 tasmāniviṣayatvameva

##
 atha ārṣajñānasya kāraṇaviṣayapramāṇanirūpaṇārtham * āmnāyavidhāta m * ityādi prakaraṇam 
_
 āmnāyo vedaḥ śrutismṛtilakṣaṇaḥ 
_
 tasya vidhātāraḥ katāraḥ 
_
 teṣāmṛṣīṇāmutpadyate * yat prātibhaṃ jñānam * iti pratibhayā kārāvaśeṣeṇa nirvatitama 
_
 yathātmanivedanam * yathā tasya padārtha mā svarūpaṃ tanivedanama tadālambanamutpadyate * tad ārṣamityācakṣate

 keṣvartheṣūtpadyate 
_
 * atītānāgatavartamāneṣu * 
_
 kiviśiṣṭeṣu

 * atīndriyeṣu dharmādiṣu * ādipadena paramāṇvādergrahaṇamiti

 * granthopanibadveṣvanupanibaddheṣu ca * granthopanibaddheṣu ātmādiṣu

 kutaḥ kāraṇādeṣu yathārthavijñānam

 * ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāt * asamavāyinaḥ   dharmaviśeṣācca * nimittāditi 
_
 tatta prastāreṇa ṛṣīṇāma tastadārṣam

 tattu kadācideva laukikānāmapyarṣīṇāmevaṃvidhaṃ vijñānamastīti

 kima smadādīnāṃ

 tra pramāṇamityāha * kadācideva lokikānām * tat prātibha jñānamiti

 na cendriyaja tat

##
 atha bāhyendriyāṇāṃ vyāpārāsambhave 'pi antaḥkaraṇasya vyāpārāt pratyakṣaphalatvam 
_
 sambandho 'pi indriyeṇa saha bhrātuḥ saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇaviśeṣya bhāvaḥ

 tathāhi 
_
 tadviśiṣṭamātmānaṃ deśaṃ kālaṃ vā ālambyotpadyate jñāna metad ityuktaṃ paraiḥ

 taccāsat 
_
 asyāparokṣatvānupa

 api tu   hṛdayaṃ me kathayatīti * brūte

##
 siddhadarśanaṃ vidyāntaramiṣṭaṃ paraistaniṣedhārthamāha * siddhadarśanaṃ na śānāntaram * iti 
_
 ārṣajñānānantaramasya antarbhāvanirūpaṇam ārṣe 'pyanta nāvātham 
_
 yat siddhānāṃ darśanamutpadyate tatpratyakṣameva

 keṣvartheṣu 
_
 * sūkṣma pāhatāvaprakṛṣṭeṣu * iti

 sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ

 vyavahitā nāgabhavanādayo dādāndriyāpekṣayā

 muktātmavyavacchedārthaṃ * dṛśya *ṇām * iti

 cid añjanādiviyuktāḥ pratyakṣeṇāpyupalabhyante

##
atha jyotiṣāmayanaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāṇināṃ śubhamaśubhaṃ vā bhaviṣyatīti jñānaṃ

yad vā divyāntarikṣabhaumānāṃ surasiddhamanuṣyāṇāṃ prāṇināṃ

##
 atha buddheranantaraṃ sukhasya kāryakāraṇasvarūpopadarśanārtham * anugrahalakṣaṇa sukham * ityādi

āsattirabhiṣvaṅa gaḥ

 nayanādiprasāda prasannatā

##
 * yattu viduṣāmasatsu viṣayānusmaraṇecchāsaṅkalpeṣa * viṣayānus raṇañcecchā ca saṅkalpaśceti tathoktāḥ

 teṣvavidyamāneṣvāvirbhavati tadupādaka meva

##
 duḥkhanirūpaṇārthamāha * upaghātalakṣaṇam * upaghātasvarūpaṃ duḥkhamiti

 tyata'neneti upahatamātmānaṃ manyata iti

 kāraṇamāha * viṣādyanabhi viṣayasānnidhye sati

 tasmādadharmāpekṣādityādipadena dikkālāde m

 paghātadanyānāṃ nimittaṃ kāraṇam

 taditarasmād bhedakamiti jñeyam 
_
 laghu sādiṣviti kāryanirūpaṇam 
_
 amarṣo 'sahiṣṇutā 
_
 upahatirupaghāto lālambanaṃ jñānamiti 
_
 dainyaṃ dīnarūpatā daḥkhātpadyata iti 
_
 tadetada māraṇatvād itarasmāda bhedakamiti jñeyam 
_
 * atīteṣu sarpavyāghracaurā * duḥkhasādhaneṣu 
_
 * smṛtijam 
_
 anāgateṣu saṅkalpajamiti

##
 icchāyāḥ kāryakāraṇasvarūpanirūpaṇārthaṃ * svārthaṃ parārtha vā * ityādi 
_
 aprāpte vastuni prārthanārūpatvādiccheti 
_
 svārthaṃ parārthaṃ veti vipratipatti nirāsārthaṃ vibhāgakathanam 
_
 na kevalaṃ svārthameva parārthamapi 
_
 utpatti kāraṇamāha * sā cātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāt * asamavāyikāraṇādutpadyate 
_
 kimapekṣāt 
_
 * sukhādyapekṣāt smṛtyapekṣād vā * iti

_
 śuddhābhisandhirdhamaheturduṣṭābhisandhi ścādharmaheturiti

##
 anye 'pi guṇāḥ kāmādayaḥ santi ca śabde 
_
te ca kiṃ na sucitā iti codyasya parihārārthamantarbhāvaṃ nirūpayati * kāmo 'bhilāṣo rāgaḥ saṅkalpaḥ kāruṇyaṃ
vairāgyam upadhā bhāva ityevamādaya icchābhedāḥ * tadviśeṣā iti
_
 maithunecchā kāmaḥ 
_
 tatsadbhāve kāmīti vyapadeśāt 
_
 necchāmātramiti 
_
 abhyava haraṇecchā abhilāṣaḥ 
_
 abhilāṣalakṣaṇecchā 
_

_
 tadicchā abhilāṣa iti cānye 
_
 * punaḥ punarviṣayānurañjanecchā rāgaḥ * tena hi satā rāgīti vyapadeśāt 
_
 anāsanna kriyāyām anāgatakriyāyāmicchā saṅkalpaḥ 
_
 * svārthamanapekṣya paraduḥkhaprahā ṇecchā * tadvināśecchā kāruṇyam 
_
 doṣadarśanād viṣayeṣu parityāgecchā vairāgyam 
_
 tat sadbhāve viraktavyavahārāt 
_
 * paravañcanecchā upadhā 
_
 antarnigūḍhecchā bhāvaḥ * iti 
_
 yadyapi icchā sarvā antarna bāhyeti 
_
 tathāpi iyamanyāpekṣayā kathañcid vijñāyata ityantanigūḍhetyucyate

 * cikīrṣā jihīretyādikriyābhedādicchābhedā bhavanti * kartumicchā cikīrṣā 
_
 hartumicchā jihīrṣeti

##
 dveṣanirūpaṇārthamāha * prajvalanātmakaḥ prajvalanasvarūpo dveṣaḥ 
_
 * yasmin sati prajvalitamivātmānaṃ manyate 
_
 sa dveṣaḥ 
_
 iti pūrvasya vivaraṇam 
_
 * sa cātmanasoḥ saṃyogāt 
_
 asamavāyikāraṇāt 
_
 * duḥkhāpekṣāt smṛtyapekṣād vā * ātmanyutpadyata iti 
_
 * prayatnasmṛtidharmādharmahetuḥ * iti kāryanirūpaṇam

 yathā hi dveṣād vadhādau pravarttamānasyādharmo bhavatyevaṃ yajanādau pravarttamānasya dharmo 'pīti

 bhedanirūpaṇārthamāha *drohaḥ krodho manyurakṣamā amarṣa iti dveṣabhedāḥ * tadviśeṣā iti

##
pa karaṇam 
_
 nanvete sukhaduḥkhecchādveṣāḥ kathaṃ vijñānād vyatiricyante 
_
 samānakāraṇa janyatvād antarmukhākāratayā pratīyamānatvācceti kāraṇabhedena hi padārthā bhidyanta ityuktam 
_
 taduktam tadatadrūpiṇo bhāvāstadatadrūpahetujāḥ 
_
 tatsukhādi kimajñānaṃ vijñānābhinnahetujam 
_
 iti 
_

_
 kecid bhāvastadrūpiṇo dhānyādirūpiṇaḥ

##
naitadevam 
_
 abhede sādhye samavāyya samavāyinimittāpekṣayāpi samānakāraṇajanyatvasya vyabhicārāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 ekasmāt samavāyikāraṇādutpadyante pākajāḥ parasparaṃ vibhinnāśceti 
_
 asamavāyikāraṇantu pārthivaparamāṇvagnisaṃyogasteṣāmeka eva 
_
 tathā eko 'pyuṣṇasparśasteṣāṃ nimittakāraṇamiti 
_
 tadapekṣayāpi vyabhicāraḥ 
_
 sāmagracapekṣayā tvasiddhaṃ samānakāraṇajanyatvam 
_
 tasyāḥ pratikāryaniyatatvāt 
_
 uktañca ekatra sragādyapalakṣitā sāmagrī kāraṇam 
_
 anyatrānyathābhateti 
_
 tathā pratiniyatajātaḥ prāgabhāvasya cānupraveśe sarvatra sāmagrībhedo bhavatyeveti 
_
 antarmukhākāratayā pratīyamānatvañca jñānadharmarvyabhicārīti 
_
 asti ca dharmadharmiṇorbheda ityuktam 
_
 tathā jñānasyānutpattivināśābhyāṃ vyabhicāraḥ 
_
 tayorantarmukhākāratayā pratāya mānatvam 
_
 na ca bodharūpatetyalamatiprasaṅgena 
_

##
 atha prayatnasya kāraṇasvarūpavibhāganirūpaṇārthamāha * prayatnaḥ saramma utsāha iti paryāyāḥ * lakṣaṇam 
_
 asādhāraṇatvāt 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 prayatna itara smād bhidyate 
_
 anādikālapravāhāyātetthambhūtaparyāyābhidheyatvāt 
_
 yastu 
_
 bhidyate 
_
 na cāsāvevam 
_
 yathā rūpādiriti 
_
 sa dvividhaḥ kāraṇabhedādityāha * jīvanapūrvaka icchādveṣapūrvakaśca jīvanaṃ pūrva kāraṇamasyeti jīvanapūrvakaḥ 
_
 sa kathaṃ vijñāyata ityāha * suptasya prāṇāpānasantānaprerakaḥ * iti 
_
 suptasya prāṇāpānasantānakriyā 
_
 sā prayatnakāryā śarīra kriyātvāt 
_
 jāpa vasthāyāṃ prāṇakriyādivaditi 
_
 na paraṃ prāṇādisantānaprerakaḥ * prabāyakā 
_
 cāntaḥkaraṇasyendriyāntareṇa prāptihetuḥ * iti 
_
yathā hi prabāyata yenaivendriyeṇopalambhastenaiva sambandhārthamantaḥkaraṇasya nirindriyātmā vartamānasyāvaśyaṃ karmābhyupeyam
_
 tacca prayatnakārya parigṛhītāntara karmatvāt 
_
 jāgradavasthāyāṃ tatkarmavat 
_
 ata eva nādṛṣṭasyaivātra kāraṇa anamānena prayatnakāryatvopalabdheḥ 
_
 kāraṇāntarāsambhave cādṛṣṭasyavānā kāraṇatvamiṣyata iti 
_
 
##
sthite hi sadbhāve jīvanapūrvakasyotpattikāraṇamāha * ātmamanasoḥ pāgāt * asamavāyikāraṇāda viśiṣṭadharmādharmāpekṣādatpattiriti
_
 itarastu raṇadvaṣapūrvakaḥ * hitāhitaprāptiparihārasamarthasya vyāpārasya * kāyikavyāpārasya hetuḥ 
_
 tathā * śarīravidhārakaśca * 
_
 tena hi pratibaddhaṃ śarīre gurutvaṃ na patanamārabhate 
_
 tasyotpattikāraṇamāha * ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāta * asamavāyi kāraṇāt 
_
 * icchāpekṣāda dveṣāpekṣād votpadyate * iti

##
 gurutvasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthaṃ garutvaṃ jalabhamyoḥ' ityādi prakaraṇama 
_
 pratyakṣatve sati patanakarmakāraṇatvād gurutvam itarasmād miyata 
_
 padāpekṣaṃ vā lakṣaṇam 
_
 jā gurutvam 
_
 raso 'pi jalabhūna vā 
_
 ca kāraṇātiśayana bhāvena pātātiśayābhā nāstīti na rasaḥ kāraṇa patanakarmakāraṇamityapratyakṣagrahaṇam 
_
 jalabhamyoti āśrayānarū vā lakṣaṇam 
_
 jalabhamyoreva vartamānatve sati patanakarmakāraṇatvāda 
_
 raso 'pi jalabhamyoreva vartate 
_
 na tu patanakāraṇama 
_
 abhyupagame 'kāraṇātiśayena kāryātiśayasya anyatropalabdhaḥ pāṣāṇāde rasātiśayā tātiśayābhāvaḥ 
_
 pippalyādau ca tatsadbhāvena sadabhāvaḥ syāta 
_
 sa śati na rasaḥ kāraṇaṃ patanotpattau 
_
 rūpādeśca kāraṇatve analādāvapi pat pātaḥ syāt 
_
 na cāstītyato rūpādivyatiriktaṃ kāraṇamanumīyata maha* patanakarmānameyama iti 
_
 ādyasya hi patanakarmaṇo 'samavāyi gurutvam 
_
 dvitīyādestu saṃskāro 'pīti 
_
 sa cāsau jalabhūmyoreva kāraṇaṃ gurutvam 
_
 dvitīyādava vartate 
_
 pratyakṣatāprasaṅgāt 
_
 atha ca tat pṛthivyādigurutvaḥ 
##
 nanu tvagindriyasya vyāpārāta pañcapalaṃ daśapalamiti pratibhāsanād   satyakṣam 
_
 na 
_
 tvagindriyeṇa sambandhopapatteḥ pṛthivyādigarutvasyāpi pratyakṣatāprasaṅgāt 
_
 atha ādheyagatameva gurutvaṃ paricchinatti tvagindriyam 
_
 na cavyādigurutve 'stīti 
_
 nanvevamapi makṣikādigurutvaṃ paricchindyāt 
_
 tasyāpyādheyagatatvāditi 
_
 na ca tasya aviśiṣṭatvādaparicchedaḥ 
_
 pratyakṣadravyasa mavāyasyāviśeṣāt 
_
 atha adhogatihetutvaṃ vaiśiṣṭayam 
_
 tarhi tvagindriyasamba ndhena adhogativiśeṣamupalabhamānasya pañcapalaṃ daśapalamityānumānika eva pratyayaḥ 
_
 
##
 atha daśapalaistantubhirārabdhe paṭe gurutvātiśayasyānupalabdheḥ 
_
 kāraṇa eva gurutvam 
_
 na tu kārye 
_
 tadasat 
_
 ubhayatrāpi pātopalabdheḥ 
_
 na ca svagatagurutvā bhāve 'pi āśrayāntaragurutvādeva patanam 
_
 vāyvāderapi pātaprasaṅgāt 
_
 tasmāduḥ bhayatrāpi kāryeṇa sadbhāvasiddhergurutvamastīti 
_
 avanativiśeṣānupalambhaśca kārye makṣikādigurutvasamparkeṇāpi samāna iti 
_
 tathāhi 
_
 tantuṣu mīyamāna makṣikādisamparke 'pi avanativiśeṣā nopalabhyante 
_
 na ca tadgurutvasyāsattva mityalam

##
 atha gurutvasya pātahetutve kimiti sarvadā pāto na bhavati 
_
 pratibandhā dityāha * saṃyogaprayatnasaṃskāravirodhi * iti 
_
 vṛntaphalasaṃyogena pratibaddha na phale patanamārabhate 
_
 prayatnapratibandhād ākāśāvasthiteṣu śakuniṣu gurutvaṃ na patanaṃ karoti 
_
 dhanunikṣipteṣu śareṣu gurutvaṃ na patanaṃ karoti vegākhyasaṃskā pratibandhāt 
_
 eṣāmapāye phalādiṣu pātadarśanāt

##
 * tasya cābādiparamāṇurūpādivannityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ iti 
_
 abādayaśca te paramāṇavaśceti tathoktāḥ 
_
 tatparamāṇurūpādīnāmiveti 
_
 yathā āpyaparamāṇurūpādīnāmaniṣpadyamānatvānnityatvam 
_

_

##
 dravatvasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthamāha*dravatvaṃ syandanakarmakāraṇam iti 
_
 syandana   vakṣyamāṇam 
_
 tatkāraṇaṃ dravatvamityukte vegena vyabhicāraḥ 
_
 tadarthaṃ tridravya ta 
_
 tathāpi nidravyavattitvaṃ vegasyāpi sambhavatīti niyameneti padamūhyam 
_
 rūpantu niyamena tridravyavṛtti 
_
 na tu syandanakamakāraṇam 
_
 sarasmā dbhidyate 
_
 niyamena tridravyavṛttitve sati syandanakarmakāraṇatvāditi

##
 tattu dvividhamiti vibhāgaḥ 
_
 kena rūpeṇa 
_
 sāṃsiddhikaṃ naimittika pati 
_
 tayoḥ parasparaṃ vailakṣaṇyanirūpaṇārthamāha * sāṃsiddhikamapāṃ viśeṣaguṇaḥ 
_
 naimittika pṛthivītejasoḥ sāmānyaguṇaḥ * iti parasparabhedaḥ 
_
 * sāṃsiddhi tya gurutvavannityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ iti 
_
 yathā gurutvaṃ nityeṣvaniṣpadya mānatvānnityama anityeṣa niṣpatteranityaṃ kāraṇaguṇapūrvakamāśrayavināśācca vinaśyati 
_
 evaṃ sāṃsiddhikadravatvamapītyatideśārthaḥ

##
 nanu cāyuktametad apāṃ sāṃsiddhikadravyatvamiti 
_
 himakarakādāvanupa bhāt 
_
 * tadāha saṅghātadarśanāt sāṃsiddhikatvamayuktamiti cet 
_
 * naitadevam 
_
 patra salile sāṃsiddhikadravatvasyopalabdheḥ 
_
 āpyaparamāṇuṣu tatsadbhāvasiddhau himakarakādo tasyānatpādāta pratibandhakamastīti niścīyate 
_
tacca anyasyāna palambhād divyatejaḥsaṃyoga evetyāha   divyatejaḥsaṃyuktānāmāpyānāṃ
paramāṇūnāṃ raspara saṃyogo dravyārambhakaḥ *
_
 sa ca * saṅghātākhyaḥ 
_
 tena paramāṇudravatvasya tibandhāt kārye himakarakādau dravatvānutpattiḥ * iti 
_
 tejaḥsadbhāvastu sphoṭādikāryānumeyaḥ 
_
 tathā ca himakarakāsambandhādupalabhyate sphoṭādilakṣaṇaṃ kārya śarīre vṛkṣādau ca dāha iti 
_
 vilayanañcāsya divyatejaḥsambandhāt 
_
 avayave kriyā

 tato vibhāgastasmāt saṃyoganivṛttau dravyavināśe sati paramāṇavaḥ kāryamārabhante

 tatra ca divyatejaḥsaṃyogasya pratibandhakasya nivṛtteḥ paramāṇudravatvaṃ kārye dravatvamārabhate

##
 na cedaṃ naimittikam 
_
 sarpirādāviva punaḥ saṃgrahānupalabdheḥ 
_
 yathāhi naimittikadravatvaṃ sarpirādāviti drutasya saṃgrahaḥ 
_
 tathehā'pi syāt 
_
 na caitadastīti 
_
 * naimittikañca pṛthivītejasoragnisaṃyogajam * 
_
 kathamityavyutpannapraśnaḥ 
_
 tatrāha sarpirādīnāṃ kāraṇeṣvityādipadena sūtroktānāṃ saṃgrahaḥ 
_
 tathāhi sapirjatumadhūcchiṣṭānāṃ pārthivānāmagnisaṃyogād dravatvamadbhiḥ sāmānyam 
_
 trapusosaloharajatasuvarṇānāṃ taijasānāmagnisaṃyogādravatvamadbhiḥ sāmānyamiti 
_
 ataḥ sapirādikāraṇeṣu ca paramāṇuṣvagnisaṃyogā pekṣā vegāpekṣāt karmotpattau satyantato vibhāgā jāyante 
_
 tebhyo vibhāgebhyoṃ dravyārambhakasaṃyogavināśaḥ 
_
 tataḥ kāryadravyanivṛttistasyāñca satyāmagni saṃyogād auṣṇyāpekṣāt svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu dravatvamutpadyate 
_
 paramāṇavaḥ sabhavāyikāraṇam

##
agnisaṃyogo 'samavāyikāraṇamuṣṇasparśī nimittakāraṇa miti 
_
 tato 'nantaramutpannadravatveṣu * bhogināmadṛṣṭāpekṣādātmāṇusaṃyogāt * karmotpadyata iti 
_
 paramāṇuḥ samavāyikāraṇam 
_
 ātmāṇusaṃyogo 'samavāya kāraṇam 
_
 bhogināmadṛṣṭo nimittakāraṇamiti 
_
 tato vibhāgebhyaḥ prāktana saṃyogavināśe sati tebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ paramāṇvantareṇa saṃyogā jāyante

 tebhyaḥ saṃyogebhyo dvacaṇukāṇyutpadyante 
_
 tadādikrameṇa vyaṇukādikāryamutpadyata

tasmiśca dvayaṇukādau * rūpādyutpattisamakālaṃ kāraṇaguṇapūrvakrameṇa dravatvamutpadyara iti * pākajotpattinyāyo 'tra draṣṭavyaḥ

 etāvāṃstuviśeṣaḥ

##
 snehasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthaṃ * sneho 'pāṃ viśeṣaguṇaḥ saṅgrahamajādihetuḥ * śata

 apāṃ viśeṣaguṇo rūpādirapīti saṅgrahamṛjādiheturiti padam 
_
 saṅgrahaḥ piṇḍīkaraṇam

 mṛjā tu viśadatvam

 nanu snehasyābhinavapallavādāvupalambhād udakaviśeṣaguṇatvamasiddham

_
 sayuktasamavāyenopalambhāt

 saṃyukta hi pallavādinā udakaṃ tatsamaveta nahā gṛhyate

 tadapāye tasyānupalabdheḥ

 tathā snānottarakālaṃ keśādau 'nagdhapratyayadarśanāt

 nityeṣu nityo 'nityeṣu kāraṇaguṇapūrvaḥ

 āśrayavināśād vinaśyatīti

##
 saskāranirūpaṇārthamāha * saṃskārastrividhaḥ * 
_
 kena rūpeṇa 
_
 vego bhāvanā tasthāpakatveneti 
_
 vibhāga evāsādhāraṇatvāllakṣaṇamiti 
_
 tallakṣaṇa citryajñāpanārthametat 
_
 tatra vegasya samānajātīyāt bhedamāśrayañca nirūpa nāha* mūrtimatsū * ityādi 
_
 mūrtimatsu dravyeṣu 
_
 na jñāyate kiyatsu 
_
 tadarthaṃ * pañcasu *

 tadarthaṃ * mūrtimatsu * ityāśrayanirūpaṇam

 vā saṃskāratve sati pañcasu mūrtimatsveva vartamānatvād vega iti lakṣaṇam

##
 kāraṇamāha nimittaviśeṣāpekṣāt karmaṇo jāyate iti 
_
 saṃyogavibhāgayoḥ tvamiti nimittaviśeṣāpekṣāditi viśeṣaṇam 
_
 nimittaviśeṣo nodanā atisaṃyuktasaṃyogāḥ 
_
 tadapekṣāditi 
_
 karma asamavāyikāraṇam 
_
 svakāraṇa sapā nodanādinimittakāraṇama 
_
 vegādhārastū samavāyikāraṇamitya raṇatvāllakṣaṇaṃ cedama 
_
 kāryasāha niyatāyāṃ diśi kriyāprabandhasya kriyāsantānasya heturiti 
_
 
##
 nanu cāyuktametat 
_
 aniyatadigadeśasya bhramaṇākhyasyāpi karmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvāt 
_
 satyametat 
_
 tathāpyadoṣaḥ 
_
 niyatadikriyāprabandhasyaiva heturityavadhāra ṇānabhyupagamāt 
_
 so 'pi niyatāyāmeva diśi kriyāprabandha iti cānye 
_
 ani yatadikriyāprabandhaheturityavadhāraṇasyātra pūrvarūpatāṃ manyamānā vyākhyāntara kurvate 
_
 tasya vināśakāraṇamāha * sparśavadravyasaṃyogaviśeṣavirodhī * iti 
_
 sparśavadravyasaṃyogamātravirodhitve vāyusaṃyogena virodhādiṣorgamanaṃ na syāt 
_
 taddhetoāgasya vināśāditi viśeṣagrahaṇama 
_
 kaṭhināvayavasaṃyogenādāvāpa tadvināśopalabdheḥ 
_
 
##
 nanvevamapyākāśe prakṣiptasyeṣonibiḍāvayavasaṃyogasya vegavināśakasyā bhāvādapātaḥ syāt 
_
 na 
_
 anekakāryakaraṇe sparśavadravyasaṃyogamātreṇāpi vinā śasyānvayavyatirekābhyāmupalambhāt 
_
 tathā ca kṣiptasyeṣorvegavināśopalabdha ravaśyaṃ kāraṇamabhidheyam 
_
 nirhetukavināśapratiṣedhāt 
_
 ato vāyusaṃyogenāpyaneka kāryakaraṇe sati virudhyate 
_
 adṛṣṭaprakṣayād veti 
_
* kvacit kāraṇaguṇapūva prakrameṇotpadyate * yathā parvatasrotasāmadhaḥpatatāṃ
saṃyoge satyekasminnudaka samutpanne rūpādivat kāraṇavegād bego 'pīti

##
 bhāvanāsaṃjñakastvātmaguṇatvāditarasmād bhidyate 
_
 na ca buddhayādiā' bhicāraḥ 
_
 saṃskārasya sato 'vāntaraviśeṣanirūpaṇāt 
_
 * smṛtipratyabhijñānahara iti kāryanirūpaṇam

 sadbhāve pramāṇañceti

##
 nāśakāraṇamāha * jñānamadadaḥkhādivirodhī * iti 
_
 jñānaṃ pratipakṣajñānaṃ vivakṣitam 
_
 tena virudhyate 
_
 yathā ātmādijñānajanitaḥ saṃskāro nairātmyā camyāseneti 
_
 tasmin sati tatrāsmaraṇāt 
_
 svamadena virodhaḥ 
_
 bālāvasthānubhavajanitasaṃskārasya punaryavāvasthāyāṃ viṣayābhibhūtasya tatrāsmaraṇāt

 tena satā tatrāsmaraṇāt 
_
 ādipadena tu krodhāderapi saṃskāranivartakatvamuktam

##
tasyotpattikāraṇamāha paṭavabhyāsādarapratyayebhyo jātastatpratyayaja ta 
_
 paṭupratyayāpekṣādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇādātmanyāścarye 'rthe saṃskāro jāyate 
_
 * yathā dākṣiṇātyasyoṣṭradarśanāt 
_
 sa cātiśayena smṛtiheturbhavatīti 
_
* vidyāśilpavyāyāmādiṣvabhya mānaṣu tasminnevārthe pūrvapūrvasaṃskāramapekṣamāṇādattarottarasmāt
pratyayā manasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskārātiśayo jāyate
_
 pūrvapūrvasaṃskārāpekṣo hi sarāttarapratyayo 'bhyāsaḥ 
_
 tamapekṣamāṇādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇā māna saskārātiśayo jāyate * 
_
 tatra vidyāyāma upādhyāyoccaritapadaśravaṇe ka saṃskāraḥ 
_
 pūnarvivakṣādikrameṇa svayamuccāraṇe sati tu jñānaṃ pūrva skārāpekṣaṃ saṃskārāntaramārabhate 
_
punastaduccāraṇe sati tajjñānaṃ pūrvasaṃskā pakṣa saṃskārāntaramārabhata ityevaṃ
tricaturādiparivarttane satyantyapadānubhavāt saskārāpekṣāta saṃskārātiśayo jāyate
_
 etaccāvaśyamabhyupeyam 
_
 
##
anyathā savayathya syāt 
_
 na cātiprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 adṛṣṭasya vyavasthāhetutvāt 
_
 na ca bhāsta sarvatra sadabhāvaḥ 
_
 kāryasya smaraṇasya sarvatrānupalabdheḥ 
_
 yatra hi ṇamāsta tatraiva pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaṃ jñānaṃ saṃskāramārabhata iti 
_
 āntare pāsa pūrvapūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaṃ niyatārthasmaraṇameva saṃskāramārabhata iti yam 
_
 evaṃ śilpe 'pyapādhyāyalikhitacitradarśanāta saṃskāraḥ 
_
 punaḥ svayaṃ pādhopalabhate 
_
 tadanubhavaḥ pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaḥ saṃskārāntaramārabhate 
_
 punaḥ svayaṃ khatvopalabhate 
_
 tadanabhavaḥ pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaḥ saṃskārāntaramārabhate 
_
 ityevaṃ dvinyādiparivarttanena saṃskārātiśayaḥ 
_
vyāyāme 'pi upādhyāyena dhanurvedapari paṭhitanyāyena prayukteṣūpalambhādupajāte saṃskāre punastadanusāritayā svayaṃ
prayukta tadanubhavena pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣeṇa saṃskārāntaramārabhyate
_
 punastathaiva prayoge sati tadanubhavena pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣeṇānyaḥ saṃskāra ityevamantyānubhavāt saṃskārātiśaya iti 
_

##
 ādarapratyayajasaṃskāramāha * prayatlena manaḥ cakṣuṣi sthāpayitvā apūrvamartha didṛkṣamāṇasya   iti 
_
 draṣṭumicchato vidyutsampātadarśanena tulyaṃ vartate 
_
 iti tadarśanavadādarapratyayaḥ 
_
 tamapekṣamāṇādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇā dātmani saṃskārātiśayo jāyate 
_
 * yathā devahrade sauvarṇarājatapadmadarśanā *   diti 
_
tatra hi sauvarṇarājatapatrayorutthānamāgamāllokapravādato vā
samupalabhya punaviśiṣṭayātrāsamaye prayatnena saṃskārātiśayo bhavatīti

##
 sthitisthāpakastu saṃskāratve sati sparśavatsveva dravyeṣu vartamānatvā ditarasmāda bhidyate 
_
 kiṃ bhūteṣu 
_
 * dhanāvayavasanniveśaviśiṣṭaṣu iti 
_
 ghanāśca te avayavāśca 
_
 teṣāṃ sanniveśo racanāviśeṣaḥ 
_
 ghana iti sanniveśasya vā viśeṣaṇam 
_
 tadviśiṣṭeṣu

 * kālāntarāvasthāyiṣu svāśrayamanyathākṛtaṃ yathāvat sthāpayati * ityataḥ sthitisthāpakaḥ

##
 sadbhāve pramāṇamāha sthāvarāśca jaṅgamāśceti tathoktāsteṣāṃ vikāreṣu dhanuḥśākhādantaśṛṅgāsthiṣu 
_
 sūtravastrādiṣu ca bhagneṣu saṃvartiteṣu piṇḍī kṛteṣu tasya kārya saṃlakṣyate 
_
 tathāhi dhanuṣi śākhādī ca ākarṣaṇakarmaṇyupa jāte nodanādibhyastannivṛttāvapi karmopalambhādavaśyamasamavāyikāraṇaṃ vācyam 
_
 vastunastadantareṇānutpatteḥ 
_
 na ca nodanāderanyatamaḥ sambhāvyata ityanyenāsama vāyikāraṇena bhavitavyam 
_
 kriyāvibhāgayośca kriyotpattāvakāraṇatvopalambhāt 
_
 tathā tannivṛttāvapi pratibandhakābhāve sati śākhādau pūrvāvasthāvasthāpakakarmopa lambhānimittāntarameva nyāyyam 
_
 adṛṣṭa viśeṣasya tu sādhāraṇatvāt kāraṇatvaṃ na pratiṣiddhayata iti 
_
 * nityānityatvaniṣpattayo 'pyasya gurutvavad draṣṭavyā * iti 
_
yathā hi garutvaṃ nityeṣu nityamutpattivināśakāraṇābhāvādanityeṣu kāraṇapūrvakamāśraya vināśād
vinaśyati evaṃ sthitisthāpakasaṃskāro 'pīti

##
 dharmasya lakṣaṇaparokṣārthamāha * dharmaḥ puruṣaguṇaḥ * ityādi 
_
 puruṣaguṇatvaṃ buddhayādāvapītyataḥ * priyahitamokṣahetuḥ * iti 
_
 priyaṃ sukham 
_
 hitaṃ tatsādhanam 
_
 navānāmātmaviśeṣaguṇānāmatyantocchittirmokṣa iti 
_
 atheśvarajñānamapyeṣāṃ heturataḥ karturiti 
_
 yena hi kṛto dharmastatraiva priyahitamokṣahetuḥ 
_
 na caivamīśvarajñānasya 
_
 akāryatayā karturabhāvāditi 
_
 atha tattvajñānaṃ karturyathoktaphalahetustadarthamatīndriya iti 
_

##
 nanvevamapi atīndriyatve satyantyasukhasaṃvijñānavirodhitvāt 
_
 dharmaḥ itarasmād bhidyata ityukte vyabhicārābhāvād vyarthaṃ śeṣābhidhānam 
_
 na 
_
 anya svāt kartuḥ 
_
 priyahitamokṣaheturiti viśiṣṭārthakriyānirūpaṇam 
_
 puruṣaguṇa ityanyathābhāvapratiṣedhārtham 
_
 atha puruṣaguṇatve kiṃ pramāṇam 
_
 anumānamāgamaśca 
_
 tathāhi tanu bhuvanādikāryam 
_
 puruṣaguṇapūrvakam 
_
 vicitrakāryatvād 
_
 rathādivaditi 
_
 yathāhi rathādikartā bhokturabhiprāyaṃ vicitramapekṣamāṇastathaiva tadracanāṃ karoti evaṃ śarīrādikāpīti 
_
 na ca śarīrotpatteḥ pūrvamasmadādyātmani buddhayādayaḥ santi 
_
saṃskārastu smaraṇotpattāvevāvagatasāmarthya iti guṇāntaraṃ
tadgatama pakṣamāṇastadupabhoganiṣpattaye vicitraṃ śarīrādikamārabhata iti
_
 āgamastu 'yāvadātmani dharmādharmoṃ tāvadāyuḥ śarīramindriyāṇi viṣayāśceti 
_
 tathā 'kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇī'ti

##
 yeṣāntu buddhiguṇo dharmasteṣāṃ kathaṃ nākarmanimittaḥ svargaḥ 
_
tathāhi pralayāvasthāyāṃ
buddheḥ pradhāne pralīnatayā dharmādharmayoranabhivyaktī pradhānasya buddhadhādibhāvena pariṇāmo na syāt
_
 abhivyaktasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvābhyupa gamāt

 viśeṣahetvabhāvāt

 niyamahetvabhāvāt

##
 ye 'pi paramāṇurūpo dharma iti manyante 
_
 teṣāmapi tasya nityatāyāṃ sakalakriyāvilopaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 maraṇādyabhāvaśca 
_

_
 tasya paramāṇutvenotpattivināśakāraṇābhāvāt 
_
 tathā paramāṇūnāṃ dharmaśabdenābhidhāne saṃjñābhedamātrameva syāt

 atha paramāṇuguṇau dharmādhau 
_
 evamapi sarvapuruṣāṇām ekākāro bhogaḥ syāt 
_
 puṇyāpuṇyā dhikaraṇaiḥ paramāṇubhirārambhāviśeṣāt

 atha kecit puṇyādhikaraṇāḥ paramāṇavo 'nye cāpuṇyādhikaraṇāḥ

 tatrādhikaiḥ puṇyādhikaraṇairārabdhe sukhātiśayo 'dhikaiścāpuṇyādhikaraṇairduḥkhamiti cet 
_
 atrāpi tayonityatve maraṇādyabhāvaprasaṅgaḥ

 anityatvantu na yuktam

##
 anye tvanāśrito dharma iti manyante 
_
 tatrāpi anityapakṣe na kiñcid anāśritaṃ bastubhūtaṃ kārya sambhavatīti dūṣaṇam 
_
 nityapakṣe tu yāgādikriyā vilopaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 atha kriyābhivyaktaḥ kāryakāraṇaḥ 
_
 tarhi kṣaṇikatvena kriyāvināśe svargādiphalaṃ na syāt 
_
 na ca pradīpasyevābhivyañjakatvaṃ tatprakāśa katvaṃ kriyāyāḥ 
_
 tadbhāve 'pi tasyānupalambhāt 
_
 atha yāgādikriyā dharmasya sāmarthyamupajanayatīti cet 
_
 tarhi yat tat sāmarthyaṃ sa eva dharmaḥ 
_
 yatrāśritaḥ sa cātmeti saṃjñābhedamātraṃ syāt 
_
 tathā amūrtasyātmanā sambandhābhāvāt tatsambandhitvena phalābhāva ityalaṃ prasaṅgena 
_
 na ca bodhātmakameva karma 
_
 vyati rekānabhyupagame bodharūpatayā sarvatrāviśeṣeṇa jagadvaicitryāprasaṅgāt

 tasyotpattikāraṇamāha puruṣāntaḥkaraṇasaṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇādupajāyate

 naimittikānāntu parasparaṃ vyāvṛttamanuṣṭhānabhedaṃ darśayati * pākayajñasaṃsthānāma * ityādinā 
_

_

 yajñaḥ

##
 eṣāśca nityānāṃ śaktau vidyamānāyāmanuṣṭhānam 
_

 agnyādheyānāñca haviyajñasasyātām

_

##
phenapāśceti 
_
tatra vaikhānasā nāma akṛṣṭa pacyābhirauṣadhībhimabahiṣkṛtābhiragniparicaraṇaṃ
kṛtvā pañcamahāyajñakriyāṃ nivartayanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante
_
tatraudumbarā nāma prātarutthāya yāṃ diśaṃ prekṣante tadāhṛtairbadaranīvāraśyāmākairagniparicaraṇaṃ
kṛtvā pañcamahāyajñakriyāṃ nivartayanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante
_
tatra bālakhilyā nāma jaṭādharā cīravalkalasaṃvṛtāṅgāḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā kāttikyāṃ
puṣyādibhakṣa mutsṛjanta aṣṭau māsān vṛttyupārjanaṃ kṛtvā pañcamahāyajñakriyāṃ nivartayanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante
_
 tatra phenapā nāma uddaṇḍakānanmattāḥ śīrṇapatrābhibhojino yatra tatra vā vasanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante 
_
 tadevāha * valkalājinakeśaśmaśrunakha romadhāraṇaṃ vanyāmbahutātithiśeṣabhojanāni vanasthasya * iti

 na paraṃ dharmo 'dharmopyātmagaṇaḥ

##

##
pravartakāddharmāt saṃsārotpattimupadiśya nivarttakāt tannivṛttimāha * jñāna pūrvakāttu kṛtāt * iti 
_
 jñānaṃ pūrvaṃ yasya sa tathoktastasmāt 
_
 kiṃ rūpāt 
_
 *asaṅkalpitaphalāt iti 
_
 itthaṃ me śarīrendriyaviṣayāḥ sampadyantām 
_
 netthamityava na saṅkalpitaṃ phalaṃ yasya sa tathoktastasmād 
_
 viśuddhe kule janma bhavati 
_
 tasya jātasya daḥkhavigamopāyajijñāsā sampadyate kṛtaḥ sādhanādatyantaṃ duḥkha santateviyogaḥ sampadyata iti 
_
 evaṃ jijñāsorācāryopasaṅgamaḥ sampadyata 
_
 tañcopasaṅgamya duḥkhasantānavyāvṛtteruṣāyaṃ vijānāti tattvajñānācchya sampadyata iti

##
kāraṇa bhāvena kāryasyānutpatteḥ

##
khedaṃ cotpādayati

 taccotpādya paramārthaḥ sarvapadārthānāmāranā taddarśanājjātaṃ paramārthadarśana sakhaṃ karoti 
_
 tata kṛtvā nivarttate

 tadā nigata dharmādharmasamākhyātaṃ bījaṃ yasyāsau tathoktastasyātmanaḥ śarīrādinivṛttiḥ

 bījābhāvādeva punaḥ śarīrādyanatpattau satyāṃ* dagdhendhanānalavadapaśamo mākṣaḥ * iti

 pariśeṣāta santānasiviriti

) śabdasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthamāha * śabdo 'mbaraguṇaḥ * ityādi

 pratyabhijñānāderupalambhāt

##
 tadetadasat 
_
 gṛhītagrāhitvena pratyabhijñānasyāpramāṇatvāt 
_
 anadhiga tārthagantṛ pramāṇam iti sāmānyalakṣaṇābhidhānāt 
_
 athānadhigatārthe pratya bhijñānam 
_
 tanna 
_
 adṛṣṭārthatāyā mithyātvaprasaṅgāt 
_
 atha svarūpeṇādhi gatārthamapīdānīntanaṃ deśakālādyapekṣayānadhigatārthañceti 
_
 nanvevamapyubhayadoṣopanipātaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 prameyasāmagryāñca deśakālāderanta rbhāvābhyupagame 'nadhimatārthatvam 
_

_
 na ca śrotravyāpāreṇa deśakālādebrahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭam

##
pramāṇasāmagryā niyatavijñānajanakatvāt 
_
 sarvatra prameyabhedādeva vijñānabheda ityabhyupagama pratijñānamanyatāyāṃ kṣaṇikatāprasaṅgaḥ 
_
 tasmādanadhigatārthagantṛ pramāṇamityava vādino pramāṇameva pratyabhijñānam 
_
 tathā chinnodbhūtakeśanakhādiṣvanyatve 'pi sādṛśyavaśāt pratyabhijñānam 
_
 sāmānyādau cārthatathābhāvāditi dvavidhyā palabdheviśeṣānupalabdhau śabde pratyabhijñānam 
_
 na ca vyañjakānāṃ sandigdha tvādapramāṇatvam 
_
 svataḥ prāmāṇyasya pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt 
_
 anyataḥ pramāṇāda abhedapratipattyabhyupagame ca tadevāstvalaṃ pratyabhijñānena 
_
 tathā vyañjakānā kṣaṇikatayā śabdajñānānantarameva tirobhāve śabdasya 
_
 niviṣayameva syāt pratyabhijñānam 
_
 na ca vyañjakānāṃ nityatvam 
_
 sarvadā śabdavyaktiprasaṅgāt

 atha pratyabhijñānānyathānupapattyā tatkālaṃ yāvadavasthānam

 na

 vivādagocarāpannaḥ śabdo 'bhivyaktaḥ pratyabhijñānakālaṃ yāvannāvatiṣṭhata

 śabdapratyayaviṣayatvāt

 pūrvānubhūtaśabdavat

 na

##
anyatve 'pi pratyabhijñānopalabdhaḥ 
_
 yathā bālāvasthāyāmupalabdhe devadatte anyatve 'pi vṛddhāvasthāyāmupa lambhāt pratyabhijñānam 
_
 na cātrāvasthābhedamātrameva śarīrasyeti vācyam 
_
 avayavaracanāparimāṇarūpādivyatirekeṇa tadanupalambhāt 
_
 bālāvasthāyāṃ hi śithilāvayavaracanā kumārāvasthāyāṃ cānyathābhūteti tadbhedāt śarīrasya bhado 'vaśyaṃ bhāvī

##
parimāṇavati parimāṇārambhapratiṣedhāt 
_
 etad rupādiṣvapi samānam 
_
 parimāṇavināśaścā śrayavināśādeva ityanyatvameva 
_
 bālādiśarīrāṇāṃ parimāṇabhedasya kuvalayādā vanyatvenaiva vyāptatvāt 
_
 atha parasparaṃ vyāvṛtto bālādyavasthāśabdābhidheyo dhamaḥ 
_
 tasya ca vyatireke vṛddhāvasthāyāmapi bālādīnāmupalambhaḥ syāt 
_
 tenā virodhāt 
_
 virodhe vā kathamanyatvamasiddham 
_
 avyatireke 'pi teṣāmāvirbhāva tirobhāvābhyāṃ dharmiṇo 'pi tathābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ 
_
tasmāccharīrabhede 'pi sādṛśyāt sa evāyaṃ devadatta iti jñānavacchabde 'pi pratyabhijñānaṃ
bhaviṣyatīti śabdo palambhādanantaraṃ śrotravyāpāreṇaiva tadabhāvapratīterekatvagrāhakaṃ pratyabhijñānama pramāṇam

##
 karṇaśaṣkulyabhyupagame 'pi kvacicchabdasyābhivyaktau tasya vyāpakatayā sarvadeśāvasthitapuruṣāṇāmupalambhaḥ syāt 
_
 nirāvaraṇasya vyāpakatvāviśeṣāt 
_
 tathaikadeśāstasyābhivyajyante teṣāmabhede śabdasyaivābhivyaktiriti tadeva dūṣaṇam 
_
 bhede tu tadabhivyaktau kathaṃ śabdo 'rthamabhidadhyāt 
_
 yadi ca śabdaviśeṣaṇaśca śabdābhāvaḥ paricchidyate 
_
 viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvalakṣaṇenaiva sambandhenetyuktaṃ pūrvam

##
 atha śabdasyopalambhānantaramu 
_
 manupalabdhirmyañjakābhāvād nāsattvā diti cet 
_
 na 
_
 sadbhāve pramāṇābhāvād āvaraṇāderanupalambhācca 
_
 nahi aindriya kasyātīndriyamāvaraṇaṃ pramāṇena kvacidapalabdham 
_
 abhyupagame 'pi kvaci cchabdasyābhivyaktī tasya vyāpakatayā sarvadeśāvasthitapuruṣāṇāmupalambhaḥ syāt 
_
 nirāvaraṇasya vyāpakatvāviśeṣāt 
_
 yadi ca śabdātmakāniyatārthapratipāda kāścaikadeśāḥ 
_
 saṃjñābhedamātrameva 
_
 atha bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogād vegāpekṣādutpannakriyo vāyurvegavāṃśchrotradeśenāga tyābhisambadhyate 
_
 tadgatāni tu stimitavāyvantarāṇi protsārayati 
_
 tataḥ pratibandhakābhāve sati śrotraṃ śabdasya grāhakamiti
